artham dīkṣām pāpa kṣayaṅkarīm mala māyā ādi pāśānām viśleṣaḥ kriyate yayā jñānam ca janyate śiṣye sā dīkṣā bhukti mukti dā vijñātakala nāma ekaḥ dvitīyaḥ pralayākalaḥ tṛtīyaḥ sakalaḥ śāstre anugrāhyaḥ trividhaḥ mataḥ nirādhārā atha sādhārā dīkṣā api dvividhā matā nirādhārā dvayoḥ teṣām sādhārā sakalasya tu tīvra śakti nipātena nirādhārā iti sā smṛtā ācārya mūrtim āsthāya māyā tīvra ādi bhedayā śaktyā yām kurute śambhuḥ sā sādhikaraṇā ucyate iyam caturvidhā proktā sa vījā vīja varjitā sa adhikārā anadhikārā yathā tat abhidhīyate samayācāra saṃyuktā sa vījā jāyate nirvījā tu asamarthānām samayācāra varjitā sādhikārā bhavet dīkṣā sādhaka ācāryayoḥ atas nirvījāḥ dīkṣitānām tu mama putrayoḥ ekā kriyāvatī tatra kuṇḍa maṇḍala pūrvikā manaḥ vyāpāra mātreṇa yā sā jñānavatī matā ittham labdha adhikāreṇa dīkṣā acāryeṇa sādhyate skanda dīkṣām guruḥ kuryāt kṛtvā nityakriyām tatas vighnān utsārya dehalyām nyasya astram sva āsane sthitaḥ tila taṇḍula siddhārtha kuśa dūrvā akṣata udakam viśeṣa arghyam idam tatas tad ambunā dravya śuddhim tilakam sva āsana ātmanoḥ lāja candana siddhārtha bhasma dūrvā akṣatam kuśān vikirān śuddha lājān tān sa dhūpān astra mantritān śastra ambu prokṣitān etān kavacena avaguṇṭhitān nānā grahaṇa ākārān vighna ogha vinivārakān kṛtvā ṣaṭtriṃśatā dalaiḥ sapta japtam śivāstreṇa veṇīm bodha asim uttamam śivam ātmani vinyasya sṛṣṭi ādhāram abhīpsitam uṣṇīṣam śirasi nyasya alam kuryāt sva dehakam gandha maṇḍanakam svīye vidadhyāt dakṣiṇe kare śivāt abhinnam ātmānam kartāram bhāvayet yathā maṇḍale karmaṇām sākṣī kalaśe yajña rakṣakaḥ homa adhikaraṇam vahnau śiṣye pāśa vimocakaḥ sva ātmani anugṛhītā iti ṣaṣ ādhāraḥ yaḥ īśvaraḥ jñāna khaḍga karaḥ sthitvā nairṛtya abhimukhaḥ naraḥ sa arghya ambu pañcagavyābhyām prokṣayet yāga maṇḍapam catuṣpatha anta saṃskāraiḥ saṃskuryāt īkṣaṇa ādibhiḥ tān īśa diśi vardhanyām āsanāya upakalpayet nairṛte vāstu gīrvāṇān dvāre lakṣmīm prapūjayet āpye ratnaiḥ pūrayantīm hṛdā maṇḍapa rūpiṇīm siṃha sthām vardhanīm khaḍga rūpiṇīm dikṣu śakra ādi dikpālān viṣṇu antān praṇava āsanān vāhana āyudha saṃyuktān hṛdā abhyarcya sva nāmabhiḥ samādāya kumbhasya agra abhigāminīm a vicchinna payodharām bhrāmayitvā pradakṣiṇam śiva ājñām lokapālānām śrāvayet mūlam uccaran saṃrakṣata yathāyogam kumbham dhṛtvā atha tām dhāret tatas sthira āsane kumbhe sa aṅgam sampūjya śaṅkaram om haḥ astra āsanāya hūm phaṭ om om astra mūrtaye namaḥ om hūm phaṭ pāśupata astrāya namaḥ om om hṛdayāya hūm phaṭ namaḥ om śrīṃ śirase hūm phaṭ namaḥ om yaṃ śikhāyai hūm phaṭ namaḥ om gūṃ kavacāya hūm phaṭ namaḥ om phaṭ astrāya hūm phaṭ namaḥ catur vaktram sa daṃṣṭram ca smaret astram sa śaktikam sa mudgara triśūla asim sūrya koṭi sama prabham agguṣṭhena spṛśet kumbham hṛdā muṣṭyā astra vardhanīm bhuktaye muktaye tu ādau muṣṭinā vardhanīm spṛśet tad daśa aṃśena vardhanyām rakṣām vijñāpayet tatas rakṣaṇīyam jagannātha sarva adhvara dhara tvayā sthaṇḍile śivam abhyarcya sa arghya kuṇḍam vrajet naraḥ kuṇḍa vahni sruc ājya ādi prāgvat saṃskṛtya bhāvayet sṛṣṭi nyāsena vinyasya śodhya adhvānam yathāvidhi kuṇḍa mānam mukham dhyātvā hṛd āhutibhiḥ īpsitam hiraṇyā vanakā raktā kṛṣṇā tadanu suprabhā atiriktā bahu rūpā rudra indra agni āpya diṅmukhā kṣīra ādi madhuraiḥ homam kuryāt śāntika pauṣṭike abhicāre tu piṇyāka saktu kañcuka kāñcikaiḥ lavaṇaiḥ ājikā takra kaṭutailaiḥ ca kaṇṭakaiḥ bandhūka kiṃśuka ādīni vaśyā ākarṣāya homayet bilvam rājyāya lakṣma artham pāṭalān campakān api dūrvā vyādhi vināśāya sarva sattva vaśīkṛte mṛtyuñjayaḥ mṛtyujit syāt vṛddhiḥ syāt tila homataḥ āhuti aṣṭaśataiḥ mūlam aṅgāni tu daśa aṃśataḥ santarpayeta mūlena dadyāt pūrṇām yathā purā tathā śiṣya praveśāya pratiśiṣyam śatam japet mūla ādi aṣṭa astra mantrāṇām svāhā antaiḥ tarpaṇam sakṛt śikhā sampuṭitaiḥ vījaiḥ phaṭ antaiḥ ca dīpanam om hauṃ śivāya svāhā ityādi mantraiḥ ca tarpaṇam om śivāya phaṭ iti ādi dīpanam tatas śiva ambhasā sthālīm kṣālitām varma guṇṭhitām candana ādi samālabdhām badhnīyāt kaṭakam gale nyastāyām mūrti bhūtāyām bhāva puṣpaiḥ śivam yajet vastra baddha mukhāyām vā sthālyām puṣpaiḥ vahirbhavaiḥ cullyām paścima vaktrāyām nyastāyām mānuṣa ātmanā nyasta ahaṅkāra vījāyām śuddhāyām vīkṣaṇa ādibhiḥ dharma adharma śarīrāyām japtāyām mānuṣa ātmanā sthālīm āropayet astra japtām gavya ambu mārjitām gavyam payaḥ astra saṃśuddham prāsāda śata mantritam tuṇḍalān śyāmaka ādīnām nikṣipet tatra tat yathā eka śiṣya vidhānāya teṣām prasṛti pañcakam prasṛtim prasṛtim paścāt vardhayet dvi ādiṣu kramāt kuryāt ca analamantreṇa pidhānam kavaca aṇunā śiva agnau mūlamantreṇa pūrva āsyaḥ carukam pacet su khinne tatra tad cullyām śruvam āpūrya sarpiṣā svāhā antaiḥ saṃhitā mantraiḥ da tvā tapta abhighāraṇam saṃsthāpya maṇḍale sthālīm sat darbhe astra aṇunā kṛte praṇavena pidhāya asyām tad deha lepanam hṛdā su śītalaḥ bhavati evam prāpya śīta abhighāraṇam vidadhyāt saṃhitā mantraiḥ śiṣyam prati sakṛt sakṛt dharma ādi āsanake hutvā kuṇḍa maṇḍala paścime sampātam ca srucā hutvā śuddhim saṃhitayā caret dhenumudrā amṛtībhūtam sthaṇḍila īśa antikam nayet sa ājyabhāgam sva śiṣyāṇām bhāgaḥ devāya vahnaye sa ājyam mantra śatam hutvā dadyāt pūrṇām yathāvidhi maṇḍalam kuṇḍataḥ pūrve madhye vā śambhu kumbhayoḥ rudra mātṛ gaṇa ādīnām nirvartya antar balim hṛdā mama aṃśaḥ yojana āsthānam adhiṣṭhā aham adhvare śivaḥ aham iti ahaṅkārī niṣkramet yāga maṇḍapāt nyasta pūrva agra sandharbhe śastra aṇu kṛta maṇḍale praṇava āsanake śiṣyam śukla vastra uttarīyakam ūrdhvam kāyam samāropya pūrva āsyam pravilokayet caraṇa ādi śikhām yāvat muktau bhuktau vilomataḥ cakṣuṣā sa prasādena śaivam dhāma vivṛṇvatā bhasma snānāya vighnānām śāntaye pāpa bhittaye sṛṣṭi saṃhāra yogena tāḍayet astra bhasmanā punar astra ambunā prokṣya sakalīkaraṇāya tam nābheḥ ūrdhvam kuśa agreṇa mārjanīya astram uccaran dvaividhyāya ca pāśānām ālabheta śarāṇunā tad śarīre śivam sa aṅgam sa āsanam vinyaset tatas puṣpa ādi pūjitasya asya netre netreṇa vā hṛdā pradakṣiṇa kramāt enam praveśya śiva dakṣiṇam saṃhāra mudrayā ātmānam mūrtyā tasya hṛd ambuje śiva hastam pradātavyam rudra īśa pada dāyakam śiva sevā graha upāyam datta hastam śiva aṇunā śive prakṣepayet puṣpam apanīya arca kantāram tad pātra sthāna mantra āḍhyam śiva deva gaṇa anugam vipra ādīnām kramāt nāma kuryāt vā sva icchayā guruḥ śiṣya deha viniṣkrāntām suṣumṇām iva cintayet tad mūlam ātma jaṅghāyām agran ca iti śikhidhvaje śiṣyasya hṛdayam gatvā recakena śiva aṇunā purakeṇa samāgatya svakīyam hṛdya antaram śiva agninā punar kṛtvā nāḍī sandhānam īdṛśam hṛdā tad sannidhāna arthan juhuyāt āhuti trayam ittham samaya dīkṣāyām bhavet yogyaḥ bhava arcane saṃskāra dīkṣā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca vakṣye saṃskāra dīkṣāyām vidhānam śṛṇu ṣaṇmukha kusumena astra liptena tāḍayet tam hṛdā śiśum saṃhāriṇyā tat ākṛṣya pūrakeṇa hṛdi nyaset tatas vāgīśvarī yaunau mudrayā udbhava sañjñayā om hāṃ hāṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ snigdhaḥ pradakṣiṇa āvartaḥ sugandhiḥ śasyate analaḥ viparīta sphuliṅgī ca bhūmi sparśaḥ praśasyate iti evamādibhiḥ cihnaiḥ hutvā śiṣyasya kalmaṣam pāpa bhakṣaṇa homena dahet vā tam bhava ātmanā dvija tva āpādana arthāya tathā rudra aṃśa bhāvane āhāra vīja saṃśuddhau garbhādhānāya saṃsthitau śatāni pañca mūlena vauṣaṭ ādi daśa aṃśataḥ śithilībhūta bandhasya śaktau utkarṣaṇam ca yat māyā ātmanoḥ vivekena jñānam sīmanta vardhanam śiva ādi tattva śuddheḥ tu svīkāraḥ jananam matam saṃhāra mudrayā ātmānam sphurat vahni kaṇā upamam kuryāt sama vaśībhāvam tadā ca śivayoḥ hṛdi brahma ādi kāraṇā tyāga kramāt recaka yogataḥ nītvā śiva antam ātmānam ādāya udbhava mudrayā śiṣyasya hṛdaya ambhoja karṇikāyām vinikṣipet pūjām śivasya vahneḥ ca guruḥ kuryāt tadā ucitām praṇatim ca ātmane śiṣyam samayān śrāvayet tathā śiva agni guru pūjā ca kartavyā jīvita avadhi bāla bāliśa vṛddha strī bhoga bhuj vyādhita ātmanām bhūta aṅgāni jaṭā bhasma daṇḍa kaupīna saṃyamān īśāna ādyaiḥ hṛd ādyaiḥ vā parijapya yathākramāt svāhā anta saṃhita mantraiḥ pātreṣu āropya pūrvavat sampādita drutam hutvā sthaṇḍila īśāya darśayet rakṣaṇāya ghaṭa adhastāt āropya kṣaṇa mātrakam śivāt ājñām samādāya dadīta yatine guruḥ evam samaya dīkṣāyām viśiṣṭāyām viśeṣataḥ vahni homa āgama jñāna yogyaḥ sañjāyate śiśruḥ nirvāṇa dīkṣā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca atha nirvāṇa dīkṣāyām kuryāt mūla ādi dīpanam pāśa bandhana śakti artham tāḍana ādi kṛtena vā vīja garbha śikhā ardha ntu hūm phaṭ anta dhruva ādinā om om iti hṛdaye evam śiraḥ mukhe śāntike pauṣṭike ca asya vaṣaṭ anta ādinā aṇunā havanam saṃvaraiḥ kuryāt sarvatra āpyāyana ādiṣu śiṣyam sampūjya tat sūtram suṣumṇā iti vibhāvitam mūlena tad śikhābandham pādāṅguṣṭha antam ānayet saṃhāreṇa mumukṣoḥ tu badhnīyāt śiṣya kāyake puṃsaḥ tu dakṣiṇe bhāge vāme nāryāḥ niyojayet nāḍīn tu ādāya mūlena sūtre nyasya hṛdā arcayet om hāṃ varṇa adhvane namaḥ hāṃ bhavana adhvane namaḥ om hāṃ kāla adhvane namaḥ śodhya adhvānam hi sūtrake nyasya astra vāriṇā śiṣyam prokṣya astra mantritena ca puṣpeṇa hṛdi santāḍya śiṣya dehe praviśya ca caitanyam haṃsa vīja stham viśliṣyet āyudha ātmanā om hauṃ phaṭ āchidya śakti sūtreṇa hāṃ haṃ svāhā iti ca aṇunā saṃhāra mudrayā sūtre nāḍī bhūte niyojayet om hāṃ haṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ vyāpakam bhāvayet enam tanutrāṇa avaguṇṭhayet vidyā deham ca vinyasya śānti atīta avalokanam om hāṃ śānti atīta kalā pāśāya namaḥ iti anena avalokayet he tattve mantram api ekam padam varṇāḥ ca ṣoḍaśa tathā aṣṭau bhuvanāni asyām vīja nāḍī katha dvayam viṣayam ca guṇam ca ekam kāraṇam ca sadā śivam sitāyām śānti atītāyām antar bhāvya prapīḍayet om śānti atīta kalā pāśāya phaṭ guṇau mantrau tathā abja stham ekam kāraṇam īśvaram ekam ca viṣayam śāntau kṛṣṇāyām acyutam smaret tāḍayitvā samādāya mukha sūtre niyojayet vidyāyām sapta tattvāni pādānām ekaviṃśatim ṣaṭ varṇān sañcaram ca ekam lokānām pañcaviṃśatim viṣayam rudra kāraṇam antar bhāvya atiriktāyām astram ādāya dadhyāt ca padam lokānām ca kalānām ca ṣaṣṭim guṇa catuṣṭayam mantrāṇām trayam ekam ca viṣayam kāraṇam harim antar bhāvya pratiṣṭhāyām vidhāya nābhi sūtra sthām sannidhāya āhutīḥ yajet hrīṃ bhuvanānām śatam sāgram padānām aṣṭaviṃśatim vīja nāḍī samīrāṇām dvayoḥ indriyayoḥ api varṇan tattvam ca viṣayam ekaikam guṇa pañcakam hetum brahmāṇḍa mantra stham śambarāṇām catuṣṭayam nivṛttau pīta varṇāyām antar bhāvya pratāḍayet juhuyāt āhutīḥ tisraḥ sannidhāya pāvake sa vīja āyāntu dīkṣāyām samayācārayā āgataḥ iṣṭāpūrta ādi dharma artham vyatiriktam prabandhakam om śānti atīta kalā pāśāya svāhā ityādi tarpaṇam om hāṃ haṃ hāṃ śānti atīta kalā pāśāya hūm phaṭ ityādi dīpanam tat sūtram vyāpti bodhāya kalā sthāneṣu pañcasu saṅgṛhya kuṅkuma ājyena tatra sa aṅgam śivam yajet hūm phaṭ antaiḥ kalāmantraiḥ bhittvā pāśān anukramāt om hāṃ phaṭ śānti atīta kalām gṛhṇāmi badhnāmi ca ityādi mantraiḥ kalānām grahaṇa bandhana ādi prayogaḥ pāśa ādīnām ca svīkāraḥ grahaṇam bandhanam punar puruṣam prati niḥśeṣa vyāpāra pratipattaye upaveśya atha tat sūtram śiṣya skandhe niveśayet vistṛta agha pramoṣāya śatam mūlena homayet śarāva sampuṭe puṃsaḥ striyāḥ ca praṇita udare hṛd astra sampuṭam sūtram vidhāya abhyarcayet hṛdā sūtram śivena sa aṅgena kṛtvā sampāta śodhitam nidadhyāt kalaśasya adhas rakṣām vijñāpayet iti śiṣyam puṣpam kare da tvā sampūjya kalaśa ādikam maṇḍala tritayam kṛtvā mumukṣu anuttara ānanān bhuktaye pūrva vaktrān ca śiṣyān tatra niveśayet pāṇinā kuśa yuktena arcita anantara antaram aṣṭa grāsa pramāṇam vā daśana sparśa varjitam hṛdā sambhojanam da tvā pūtaiḥ ācāmayet jalaiḥ dantakāṣṭham hṛdā kṛtvā prakṣipet śobhane śubham nyūna ādi doṣa moṣāya mūlena aṣṭa uttaram śatam vidhāya sthiṇḍila īśāya sarva karma samarpaṇam pūjā visarjanam ca asya caṇḍeśasya ca pūjanam kalaśam loka palān ca pūjayitvā visṛjya ca visṛjet gaṇam agnin ca rakṣitam yadi vā āhyatas vāhyataḥ lokapālānām da tvā saṅkṣepataḥ balim bhasmanā śuddha toyaiḥ vā snātvā yā gālayam viśet gṛhasthān darbha śayyāyām pūrva śīrṣān su rakṣitān hṛdā sat bhasma śayyāyām yatīn dakṣiṇa mastakān śikhā baddha sikhānastra sapta māṇavaka anvitān vijñāya snāpayet śiṣyān tatas yāyāt punar vahis om hili hili triśūlapāṇaye svāhā pañcagavyan carum prāśya gṛhītvā dantadhāvanam samācamya śivam dhyātvā śayyām āsthāya pāvanīm saṃsmaran saṃviśet guruḥ iti saṅkṣepataḥ proktaḥ vidhiḥ dīkṣā adhivāsane nirvāṇa dīkṣā vidhānam īśvaraḥ uvāca dadhi ārdra māṃsa madya ādeḥ praśasta abhyavahāri tā gaja aśva rohaṇam svapne śubham śukla aṃśuka ādikam taila abhyaṅga ādikam hīnam homaḥ ghoreṇa śāntaye nityakarma dvayam kṛtvā praviśya makha maṇḍapam tatas saṃśodhya ca ātmānam śiva hastam tathā ātmani maṇḍale sthaṇḍile vā api prakurvīta śiva arcanam tarpaṇam pūjanam vahneḥ pūrṇa antam mantra tarpaṇam duḥkha pradoṣa moṣāya śastreṇa aṣṭa adhikam śatam hutvā sampuṭena eva vidadhyāt mantra dīpanam kṛtvā śiṣya praveśāya labdha anujñaḥ vahis vrajet kuryāt samaya vat tatra maṇḍala āropaṇa ādikam sampāta homam tad nāḍī rūpa darbha kara anugam tad sannidhānāya tistraḥ hutvā tat śikhāyām nibadhnīyāt pādāṅguṣṭha avalambitam jñeyāni bhuvanāni asyām śatam aṣṭa adhikam tatas vibhūtiḥ avyayaḥ śāstā pinākī tridaśādhipaḥ agniḥ rudraḥ hutāśaḥ ca piṅgalaḥ khādakaḥ haraḥ nairṛtaḥ māraṇaḥ hantā krūra dṛṣṭiḥ bhayānakaḥ ūrdhvāṃśakaḥ virūpa akṣaḥ dhūmra lohita daṃṣṭravān balaḥ ca atibalaḥ ca eva pāśa hastaḥ mahā balaḥ śvetaḥ ca jayabhadraḥ ca dīrghabāhuḥ jalāntakaḥ vaḍavāsyaḥ ca bhīmaḥ ca daśā ete vāruṇāḥ smṛtāḥ śīghraḥ laghuḥ vāyu vegaḥ sūkṣmaḥ tīkṣṇaḥ kṣapā antakaḥ jaṭā mukuṭa dhārī ca nānā ratna dharaḥ tathā nidhi īśaḥ rūpavān saumya dehaḥ prasāda kṛt prakāśaḥ api atha lakṣmīvān kāmarūpaḥ daśa uttare mātṛvṛttaḥ ca piṅgākṣaḥ bhūtapālaḥ balipriyaḥ anantaḥ pālakaḥ dhīraḥ pātāla adhipatiḥ tathā vṛṣaḥ vṛṣa dharaḥ vīryaḥ grasanaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ lohitaḥ ca eva vijñeyāḥ daśa rudrāḥ phaṇi sthitāḥ saṃhāraḥ ca vihāraḥ ca lābhaḥ lipsuḥ vicakṣaṇaḥ kuṣmāṇḍaḥ ca eva satyaḥ ca brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca saptamaḥ rudraḥ ca aṣṭau ime rudrāḥ kaṭāha abhyantare sthitāḥ eteṣām eva nāmāni bhuvanānām api smaret saṃstuta pūrva sthita om sākṣin om rudra antaka om pataṅga om śabda om sūkṣma om śiva sarva sarva da sarva sānnidhya kara brahma viṣṇu rudra kara om namaḥ śivāya om namaḥ namaḥ aṣṭāviṃśati pādāni vyoma vyāpi manaḥ guha vīja ākāraḥ makāraḥ ca nāḍyā viḍā piṅgalā āhvaye prāṇa apānau ubhau vāyū ghrāṇa upasthau tathā indriye pārthivam maṇḍalam pītam vajra aṅgam caturasrakam vistāraḥ yojanānām tu koṭirasya śata āhatā prathamā sarva devānām manu ādyāḥ devayonayaḥ mṛga pakṣī ca paśavaḥ caturdhā tu sarīsṛpāḥ sthāvaram pañcamam sarvam yoniḥ ṣaṣṭhī amānuṣī paiśācam rākṣasam yākṣam gāndharvam ca aindram eva ca saumyam prāṇeśvaram brāhmam aṣṭamam parikīrtitam aṣṭānām pārthivan tattvam adhikāra āspadam matam om hām hām nivṛtti kalā pāśāya phaṭ tatas om hām hām nivṛtti kalā pāśāya svāhā iti anena aṅkuśa mudrayā pūrakeṇa ākṛṣya om nivṛtti kalā pāśāya phaṭ iti anena saṃhāra mudrayā kumbhakena adhas sthānāt ādāya om om hrāṃ hāṃ nivṛtti kalā pāśāya namaḥ iti anena udbhava mudrayā recakena kumbhe saṃsthāpya om hāṃ nivṛtti kalā pāśāya namaḥ iti anena arghyam da tvā sampūjya vimukhena eva svāhā antena sannidhānāya āhuti trayam santarpaṇa āhuti trayam ca da tvā om hāṃ brahmaṇe namaḥ iti brahmāṇam āvāhya sampūjya ca svāhā antena santarpya bhāvyam tvayā anukūlena vidhim vijñāpayet iti āvāhayet tatas devīm rakṣām vāgīśvarīm hṛdā icchā jñāna kriyā rūpām ṣaḍvidhām hi eka kāraṇam pūjayet tarpayet devīm prakāreṇa amunā tatas vāgīśvarīm viniḥśeṣa yoni vikṣobha kāraṇam hṛd sampuṭa artha vīja ādi hūm phaṭ anta śara aṇunā tatas śiṣyasya caitanyam hṛdi vahni kaṇā upamam nivṛtti stham yutam pāśaiḥ jyeṣṭhayā vibhajet yathā om hāṃ haḥ phaṭ om hāṃ svāhā iti anena atha pūrakeṇa aṅkuśa mudrayā tat ākṛṣya sva mantreṇa gṛhītvā ātmani yojayet om hāṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ brahma ādi kāraṇa tyāga kramān nītvā śiva āspadam kṣipet vāgīśvarī yonau vāmayā udbhava mudrayā om hāṃ hāṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ na atra puṃsavanam strī ādi śarīrasya api sambhavāt tathā eva bhāvayet eṣām adhikāram śiva aṇunā bhogam kavaca mantreṇa śastreṇa viṣaya ātmanā śivena śrotasām śuddhim hṛdā tattva viśodhanam pañca pañcāhutīḥ kuryāt garbhādhāna ādiṣu kramāt māyayā mala karma ādi pāśa bandha nivṛttaye niṣkṛtya eva hṛdā paścāt yajeta śatam āhutīḥ mala śakti nirodhena pāśānām ca viyojanam svāhā anta āyudha mantreṇa pañca pañca āhutīḥ yajet māyā ādi antasya pāśasya sapta vāra astra japtayā om nivṛtti kalā pāśāya phaṭ bandhaka tvañca nirvartya hastābhyām ca śara aṇunā kuryāt pañca āhutīḥ da tvā pāśa aṅkuśa nivṛttaye om haḥ astrāya phaṭ prāyaścittam tatas kuryāt astra āhutibhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ atha āvāhya vidhātāram pūjayet tarpayet tathā tatas om hāṃ śabda sparśa śuddha brahman gṛhāṇa svāhā iti āhuti trayeṇa adhikāram asya samarpayet bandhāya na punar stheyam śiva ājñām śrāvayet iti tatas visṛjya dhātāram nāḍyā dakṣiṇayā śanais saṃhāra mudrayā ātmānam kumbhakena nija ātmanā visṛjya pitarā dadyāt vauṣaṭ anta śiva aṇunā pūraṇāya vidhiḥ pūrṇā nivṛttiḥ iti śodhitā īśvaraḥ uvāca hrasva dīrgha prayogeṇa nāda nāda anta saṅginā om hāṃ hāṃ ap tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam tanmātra indriya buddhayaḥ guṇatrayam ahaṅkāraḥ caturviṃśaḥ pumān iti pratiṣṭhāyām niviṣṭhāni tattvāni etāni bhāvayet pañcaviṃśati saṅkhyāni kha ādi ya anta akṣarāṇi ca pañcāśat adhikā ṣaṣṭiḥ bhuvanaiḥ tulya sañjñitāḥ amareśaḥ prabhāvaḥ ca nemiṣaḥ puṣkaraḥ api ca tathā pādiḥ ca daṇḍiḥ ca bhāvabhūtiḥ atha aṣṭamaḥ anvīśaḥ asrātikeśaḥ ca mahākālaḥ atha madhyamaḥ kedāraḥ bhairavaḥ ca eva dvitīya aṣṭakam īritam vimalaḥ ca aṭṭahāsaḥ ca mahendraḥ bhāmaḥ eva ca gokarṇaḥ bhadrakarṇaḥ ca svarṇākṣaḥ sthāṇuḥ eva ca aja īśaḥ ca eva sarvajñaḥ bhāsvaraḥ sūdana antaraḥ subāhuḥ mattarūpī ca viśālaḥ jaṭilaḥ tathā raudraḥ atha piṅgalākṣaḥ ca kāladaṃṣṭrī bhavet tatas viduraḥ ca eva ghoraḥ ca prājāpatyaḥ hutāśanaḥ kāmarūpī tathā kālaḥ karṇaḥ api atha bhayānakaḥ mataṅgaḥ piṅgalaḥ ca eva haraḥ vai dhātṛ sajñakaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ vidhānaḥ ca śrīkaṇṭhaḥ candraśekharaḥ vyāpin om arūpa om pramatha om tejaḥ om jyotiḥ om puruṣa om agne om adhūma om abhasma om anādi om nānā om dhūdhū om bhūḥ om bhuvaḥ om svar anidhana nidhana udbhava śiva śarva paramātman maheśvara mahādeva sadbhāva īśvara mahā tejaḥ yoga adhipataye muñca prathama sarva sarvesarva iti dvātriṃśat padāni vīja bhāve trayaḥ mantrāḥ vāmadevaḥ śivaḥ śikhā gāndhārī ca suṣumṇā ca nāḍyau dvau mārutau tathā samāna udāna nāmānau rasanā pāyuḥ indriye rasaḥ tu viṣayaḥ rūpa śabda sparśa rasāḥ guṇāḥ maṇḍalam vartulam tat ca puṇḍarīka aṅkitam sitam svapna avasthā pratiṣṭhāyām kāraṇam garuḍadhvajam pratiṣṭhā anta kṛtam sarvam sañcintya bhuvana ādikam om hām khīṃ hāṃ pratiṣṭhā kalā pāśāya om phaṭ pūrakeṇa aṅkuśa mudrayā samākarṣet tatas om hām pratiṣṭhā kalā pāśāya phaṭ iti anena saṃhāra mudrayā kumbhakena hṛdayāt adhas nāḍī mudrā sūtrāt ādāya om hām hām pratiṣṭhā kalā pāśāya namaḥ iti anena udbhava mudrayā recakena kumbhe samāropayet om hām pratiṣṭhā kalā pāśāya namaḥ iti anena arcayitvā sampūjya svāhā antena āhutīnām trayeṇa sannidhāya tatas om hām viṣṇave namaḥ iti viṣṇum āvāhya sampūjya santarpya viṣṇo tava adhikāre asmin mumukṣum dīkṣayāmi aham bhāvyam tvayā anukūlena viṣṇum vijñāpayet iti tatas vāgīśvarīm devīm vāgīśam api pūrvavat āvāhya abhyarcya santarpya śiṣyam vakṣasi tāḍayet om hāṃ hāṃ haṃ phaṭ śastreṇa pāśa saṃyuktam jyeṣṭayā aṅkuśa mudrayā om hāṃ haṃ hoṃ phaṭ svāhā antena hṛdā ākṛṣya tena eva puṭita ātmanā om hāṃ haṃ hoṃ ātmane namaḥ pūrvavat pitṛ saṃyogam bhāvayitvā udbhava ākhyayā om hāṃ haṃ hāṃ ātmane namaḥ deha utpattau hṛdā hi evam śirasā janmanā tathā śikhayā vā adhikārāya bhogāya kavaca aṇunā tattva śuddhau hṛdā hi evam garbhādhānāya pūrvavat śirasā pāśa śaithilye niṣkṛtya evam śatam japet evam pāśa viyoge api tatas śāstra japtayā chindyāt astreṇa kartaryā kalā vījavatā yathā om pratiṣṭhā kalā pāśāya haḥ phaṭ visṛjya vartulīkṛtya pāśa mantreṇa pūrvavat ghṛta pūrṇe śrave da tvā kalā astreṇa eva homayet astreṇa juhuyāt pañca pāśa aṅkura nivṛttaye prāyaścitta niṣedha artham tāḍanam chedanam tatra praveśam ca api yojanam ākṛṣya grahaṇam kuryāt vidyayā hṛd pradeśataḥ ātmani āropya saṅgṛhya kalām kuṇḍe niveśayet rudram kāraṇam āvāhya vijñāpya ca śiśum prati pitroḥ āvahanam tirohitām chedanam mardanam teṣām vartulīkaraṇam tathā dāham tad akṣara abhāvam prāyaścittam atha uditam rudrāṇī āvāhanam pūjā rūpa gandha samarpaṇam om hrīṃ rūpa gandhau śulkam rudra gṛhāṇa svāhā tu viśeṣaḥ syāt iti vidyā viśodhitā śānti śodhana kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca sandadhyāt adhunā vidyām śāntyā sārdham yathāvidhi śāntau tattva dvayam līnam bhāveśvara sadāśivau hakāraḥ ca kṣakāraḥ ca dvau pratiṣṭhitāḥ vyomavyāpine vyoma vyāpya rūpāya sarvavyāpine śivāya anantāya anāthāya anāśritāya dhruvāya śāśvatāya yogapīṭha saṃsthitāya nitya yogine dhyāna āhārāya iti dvādaśa pādāni alambuṣa āyasānāḍyau vāyū kṛkara karmakau guṇau sparśa ninādau dvau ekaḥ kāraṇam īśvaraḥ vidadhyāt tāḍanam bhedam praveśam ca viyojanam ākṛṣya grahaṇam kuryāt śānteḥ vadana sūtrataḥ ātmani āropya saṅgṛhya kalām kuṇḍe niveśayet īśam tava adhikāre asmin mumukṣum dīkṣayāmi aham bhavyam tvayā anukūlena kuryāt vijñāpanām iti āvāhana ādikam pitroḥ śiṣyasya tāḍana ādikam pūrvavat pitṛ saṃyogam bhāvayitvā udbhava ākhyayā śikhayā vā adhikārāya bhogāya kavaca aṇunā layāya śastramantreṇa śrotaḥ śuddhau śivena ca tattva śuddhau hṛdā hi evam garbhādhāna ādi pūrvavat varmaṇā pāśa śaithilyam niṣkṛtya evam śatam japet chindyāt astreṇa kartaryā pāśān vījavatā yathā om śānti kalā pāśāya haḥ phaṭ visṛjya vartulīkṛtya pāśa mantreṇa pūrvavat ghṛta pūrṇe kalā astreṇa eva homayet astreṇa juhuyāt pañca pāśa aṅkuśa nivṛttaye prāyaścitta niṣedhāya dadyāt aṣṭa āhutīḥ atha om haḥ astrāya phaṭ hṛdā īśvaram samāvāhya kṛtvā pūjana tarpaṇe om hāṃ īśvara buddhi ahaṅkārau śulkam gṛhāṇa svāhā niḥśeṣa dagdha pāśasya paśoḥ asya īśvara tvayā na stheyam bandhaka tvena śiva ājñām śrāvayet iti visṛjet īśvaran devam raudra ātmānam niyojayet dadyāt mūlena śiṣyasya śirasi amṛta vindukam dadyāt pūrṇām vidhāna jñaḥ niḥśeṣa vidhi pūraṇīm asyām api vidhātavyam pūrvavat tāḍana ādiakam sva vījam tu viśeṣaḥ syāt śuddhiḥ śānteḥ apīḍitā nirvāṇa dīkṣā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca sandhānam śānti atītāyāḥ śāntyā sārdham viśuddhayā om hīṃ hāṃ iti sandhānāni vyoma rūpam anātham ca syāt anāśrita naṣṭamam oṅkāra padam īśāne mantraḥ varṇāḥ ca ṣoḍaśa akāra ādi visarga antāḥ vījena deha kārakau kuhūḥ ca śaṅkhinī nāḍyau devadatta dhanañjayau śabdaḥ guṇaḥ asya avasthā tu turyātītā tu pañcamī hetuḥ sadāśivaḥ devaḥ iti tattva ādi sañcayam sañcintya śāntyatīta ākhyam vidadhyāt tāḍana ādikam kalā pāśam samātāḍya phaṭ antena vibhidya ca śikhā hṛd sampuṭībhūtam svāhā antam sṛṇimudrayā pūrakeṇa samākṛṣya pāśam mastaka sūtrataḥ asyāḥ pūjā ādikam sarvam nivṛtteḥ iva sādhayet sadāśivam samāvāhya pūjayitvā pratarpya ca sadā khyāte adhikāre asmin mumukṣum dīkṣayāmi aham bhāvyam tvayā anukūlena bhaktyā vijñāpayet iti pitroḥ āvāhanam pūjām kṛtvā tarpaṇa sannidhī hṛd sampuṭa ātma vījena śiṣyam vakṣasi tāḍayet om hāṃ haṃ phaṭ śastreṇa pāśa saṃyuktam jyeṣṭhayā aṅkuśa mudrayā om hāṃ haṃ phaṭ svāhā antena tat ākṛṣya tena eva puṭita ātmanā om hāṃ haṃ hīṃ ātmane namaḥ pūrvavat pitṛ saṃyogam bhāvayitvā udbhava ākhyayā garbhādhāna ādikam sarvam pūrva ukta vidhinā caret mūlena pāśa śaithilye niṣkṛtya eva śatam japet mala śakti tirodhāne pāśānām ca viyojane pañca pañca āhutīḥ dadyāt āyudhena yathā purā pāśān āyudha mantreṇa sa pravāra abhijaptayā chindyāt astreṇa kartaryā kalā vīja yujā yathā om hāṃ śānti atīta kalā pāśāya haḥ phaṭ visṛjya vartulīkṛtya pāśān astreṇa pūrvavat ghṛta pūrṇe kalā astreṇa eva homayet astreṇa juhuyāt pajca pāśa aṅkuśa nivṛttaye prāyaścitta niṣedha artham dadyāt aṣṭa āhutīḥ tatas sadāśivam hṛdā āvāhya kṛtvā pūjana tarpaṇe om hāṃ sadāśiva manaḥ vindu śulkam gṛhāṇa svāhā niḥśeṣa dagdha pāśasya paśoḥ asya sadāśiva bandhāya na tvayā stheyam śiva ājñām śrāvayet iti mūlena juhuyāt pūrṇām visṛjet tu sadāśivam dadyāt āpyāyanāya asya mastake arghya ambu vindukam kheditau śiṣya dīkṣāyai yat mayā pitarau yuvām kāruṇyanān mokṣayitvā tat vraja tvam sthānam ātmanaḥ śikhā mantrita kartaryā bodha śakti svarūpiṇīm śikhām chidyāt śiva astreṇa śiṣyasya catur aṅgulām om klīṃ śikhāyai hūm phaṭ om haḥ astrāya hūm phaṭ sruci tām ghṛta pūrṇāyām go viṣ golaka madhya gām saṃvidhāya astramantreṇa hūm phaṭ antena homayet om haḥ astrāya hūm phaṭ prakṣālya sruc sruvau śiṣyam saṃsnāpya ācamya ca svayam yojanikā sthānam ātmānam śastra mantreṇa tāḍayet viyojya ākṛṣya sampūjya pūrvavat dvādaśāntataḥ ātmīya hṛdaya ambhoja karṇikāyām niveśayet pūritam ājyena vihita adhomukha śrucā prasārita śiraḥ grīvaḥ nāda uccāra anusārataḥ sama dṛṣṭi śivaḥ ca antar para bhāva samanvitaḥ kumbha maṇḍala vahnibhyaḥ śiṣyāt api nija ātmanaḥ gṛhītvā ṣaḍvidha vidhānam śruc agre prāṇanāḍikam hṛdaya ādi krama uccāra visṛṣṭam mantra sañjñakam pūrakam kumbhakam kṛtvā vyādāya vadanam manāk suṣumṇā anugatam nāda svarūpan tu tṛtīyakam saptame kāraṇe tyāgāt praśānta vikharam layaḥ tad kāla vikharam ṣaṣṭham śaktyatītam ca saptamam pūrakam kumbhakam kṛtvā vyādāya vadanam manāk śanais udīrayan mūlam kṛtvā śiṣya ātmanaḥ layam hakāre taḍit ākāre ṣaḍadhvaja prāṇa rūpiṇi ukāram paratas nābheḥ vitastim vyāpya saṃsthitam tatas param hṛdayāt catur aṅgulam oṅkāram vācakam viṣṇoḥ tatas aṣṭa aṅgula kaṇṭhakam catur aṅgula tālu stham makāram rudra vācakam tadvat lalāṭa madhya stham vindum īśvara vācakam nādam sadāśivam devam brahmarandhra avasānakam divyam pipīlikā sparśam tasmin eva anubhūya ca bhāva śūnye manaḥ atīte śive nitya guṇa udaye vilīya mānase tasmin śiṣya ātmānam vibhāvayet vimuñcan sarpiṣaḥ dhārām jvālā ante api pare śive yojanikā sthira tvāya vauṣaṭ anta śiva aṇunā da tvā pūrṇām vidhānena guṇa apadānam a caret om hāṃ ātmane sarvajñaḥ bhava svāhā om hāṃ ātmane paritṛptaḥ bhava svāhā om ātmane anādi bodhaḥ bhava svāhā om hauṃ ātmane svatantraḥ bhava svāhā om hauṃ ātman alupta śaktiḥ bhava svāhā om haḥ ātmane ananta śaktiḥ bhava svāhā ittham ṣaḍguṇam ātmānam gṛhītvā paramākṣarāt tīvra aṇu śakti sampāta janita śrama śāntaye praṇamayya īśa kumbha ādīn śivāt dakṣiṇa maṇḍale saumya vaktram vyavasthāpya śiṣyam dakṣiṇam ātmanaḥ tvayā eva anugṛhītaḥ ayam mūrtim āsthāya māmakīm iti vijñāpya deveśam praṇamya ca guruḥ svayam śreyaḥ tava astu iti brūyāt āśiṣam śiṣyam ādarāt tatas paramayā bhaktyā da tvā deve aṣṭapuṣpikām īśvaraḥ uvāca atha eka tāttvikī dīkṣā laghu tvāt upadiśyate sūtrabandha ādi kurvīta yathāyogam nija ātmanā kālāgni ādi śiva antāni tattvāni para bhāvayet sama tattve samagrāṇi sūtre maṇi gaṇān iva āvāhya śivatattva ādi garbhādhāna ādi pūrvavat pradadīta tatas pūrṇām tattva vāta upagarbhitām yojanāyai śive ca anyām sthira tva āpādanāya ca da tvā pūrṇām prakurvīta śiva kumbha abhiṣecanam abhiṣeka ādi kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca śivam abhyarcya abhiṣekam kuryāt śiṣya ādike śriye kumbhān īśa ādi kāṣṭhāsu kramaśas nava vinyaset teṣu kṣārodam kṣīrodam dadhyudam ghṛtasāgaram ikṣu kādambarī svādu mastu uda anaṣṭa sāgarān niveśayet yathāsaṅkhyam aṣṭau vidyeśvarān atha ekam śikhaṇḍinam rudram śrīkaṇṭha tu dvitīyakam saptamam sūkṣma nāmānam anantam rudram aṣṭamam yāga ālayān digīśasya racite snāna maṇḍape kuryāt kara dvaya āyāmām vedīm aṣṭa aṅgula ucchritām śrīparṇa ādi āsane tatra vinyasya ananta mānasam śiṣyam niveśya pūrva āsyam sakalīkṛtya pūjayet kṣāroda anukrameṇa atha hṛdā vidyeśa śambaraiḥ kalasaiḥ snāpayet śiṣyam svadhā dhāraṇayā anvitam pūrva udita āsane śiṣyam punar pūrva vat arcayet uṣṇīṣam yogapaṭṭam ca mukuṭam kartarīm ghaṭīm akṣamālām pustaka ādi śivaka ādi adhikārakam dīkṣā vyākhyā pratiṣṭhā ādyam jñātvā adya prabhṛti tvayā su parīkṣya vidhātavyam ājñām saṃśrāvayet iti abhivādya tatas śiṣyam praṇipatya maheśvaram vighna jvālā apanoda artham kuryāt vijñāpanām yathā abhiṣeka artham ādiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham guru mūrtinā saṃhitā pāragaḥ saḥ ayam abhiṣiktaḥ mayā śiva dadyāt pūrṇām tatas śiṣyam sthāpayet nija dakṣiṇe śiṣya dakṣiṇa pāṇi sthāḥ aṅguṣṭha ādi aṅgulīḥ kramāt kusumāni kare da tvā praṇāmam kārayet amum anugrāhyāḥ tvayā śiṣyāḥ śāstreṇa su parīkṣitāḥ bhūpa vat mānava ādīnām abhiṣekāt abhīpsitam ām śrāṃ śraum paśum hūm phaṭ iti astra rāja abhiṣekataḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca abhiṣiktaḥ śivam viṣṇum pūjayet bhāskara ādikān śaṅkha bherī ādi nirghoṣaiḥ snāpayet pañcagavyakaiḥ varṣa koṭi sahasreṣu yat pāpam sma upārjitam ghṛta abhyaṅgena devānām bhasmībhavati pāvake āḍhakena ghṛta ādyaiḥ ca devān snāpya suraḥ bhavet gṛhītvā praśna sūkṣma arṇe hṛte dvābhyām śubha aśubham tribhiḥ jīvaḥ mūladhātuḥ caturbhiḥ brāhmaṇa ādi dhīḥ yat ca ādau bhūta tattva ādi śeṣe ca evam japa ādikam aśubham madhyamam madhyeṣu indraḥ triṣu nṛpaḥ śubhaḥ saṅkhyā vṛnde jīvita abdam yamaḥ abda daśa hā dhruvam kaṭhinyā japtayā spṛṣṭe go mūtra ākṛti rekhayā ārabhya ekam trikam yāvat tri catuṣka avasānakam marut vyoma marut vījaiḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi pade tathā akṣāṇām patanāt sparśāt viṣama ādau śubha ādikam ekatrika ādim ārabhya ante ca aṣṭatrikam tathā dhvaja ādyāyāḥ samāḥ hīnāḥ viṣamāḥ śobhana ādi dāḥ āi pallavitaiḥ ka ādyaiḥ ṣoḍaśa svara pūrva gaiḥ ādyaiḥ taiḥ sa svaraiḥ ka ādyaiḥ tripurā nāma mantrakāḥ hrīṃ vījāḥ praṇava ādyāḥ spuḥ namaḥ antāḥ yatra pūjane mantrāḥ viṃśati sāhasrāḥ śatam ṣaṣṭhī adhikam tatas ām hrīṃ mantrāḥ sarasvatyāḥ caṇḍikāyāḥ tathā eva ca tathā gauryāḥ ca durgāyāḥ ām śrīṃ mantrāḥ śriyaḥ tathā tathā akṣauṃ krauṃ mantrāḥ sūryasya ām hauṃ mantrāḥ śivasya ca āṃ gaṃ mantrāḥ gaṇeśasya āṃ mantrāḥ ca tathā hareḥ śata ardha eka adhikaiḥ ka ādyaiḥ tathā ṣoḍaśabhiḥ kharaiḥ ka ādyaiḥ taiḥ sa svaraiḥ sa ādyaiḥ kāntaiḥ mantrāḥ tathā akhilāḥ śata trayam ṣaṣṭi adhikam pratyekam maṇḍalam kramāt abhiṣiktaḥ japet dhyāyet śiṣya ādīn dīkṣayet guruḥ pratiṣṭhā vidhi kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca pratiṣṭhām sampravakṣyāmi kramāt saṅkṣepataḥ guha pīṭham śaktim śivaḥ liṅgam tad yogaḥ sā śiva aṇubhiḥ pratiṣṭhāyāḥ pañca bhedāḥ teṣām rūpam vadāmi te yatra brahmaśilā yogaḥ sā pratiṣṭhā viśeṣataḥ sthāpanam tu yathāyogam pīṭhe eva niveśanam utthāpanam ca sā proktā liṅga uddhāra puraḥsarā yasyām tu liṅgam āropya saṃskāraḥ kriyate budhaiḥ āthāpanam tat uddiṣṭam dvidhā viṣṇu ādikasya ca āsu sarvāsu caitanyam niyuñjīta param śivam yad ādhāra ādi bhedena prāsādeṣu api pañcadhā parīkṣam atha medinyāḥ kuryāt prāsāda kāmyayā pītā kṛṣṇā surā gandhā vipra ādīnām mahī kramāt pūrva īśa uttara sarvatra pūrvā ca eṣām viśiṣyate ākhāte hāstike yasyāḥ pūrṇe mṛd adhikā bhavet uttama antām mahīm vidyāt toya ādyaiḥ vā samukṣitām asthi aṅgāra ādibhiḥ duṣṭām atyantam śodhayet guruḥ nagara grāma durga artham gṛha prāsāda kāraṇam khananaiḥ go kula āvāsaiḥ karṣaṇaiḥ vā muhur muhur maṇḍape dvāra pūjā ādi mantra tṛpti avasānakam samīkṛtya upaliptāyām bhūmau saṃśodhayet diśaḥ svarṇa dadhi akṣataiḥ rekhāḥ prakurvīta pradakṣiṇam madhya ādi īśāna koṣṭa sthe pūrṇa kumbhe śivam yajet bāhye rakṣaḥ gaṇān iṣṭvā vidhinā diś balam kṣipet bhūmim saṃsicya saṃsnāpya kuddāla ādyam prapūjayet nidhāya gīta vādya ādi brahma goṣa samākulam pūjām kumbhe samāhṛtya prāpte lagne agnikoṣṭhake nairṛtyām kṣepayet mṛtsnām khāte kumbha jalam kṣipet siñcan sīmanta cihnāni yāvat īśāna gocaram karkara antam jala antam vā śalya doṣa jighāṃsayā khānayet bhūḥ kumārīm ced vidhinā śalyam uddharet aka ca ṭa ta pa ya śa hān mānavaḥ ced praśna akṣarāṇi tu agneḥ dhvaja ādi pātitāḥ sva sthāne śalyam ākhyānti kartuḥ ca aṅga vikāreṇa jānīyāt tat pramāṇataḥ paśu ādīnām praveśena kīrtanaiḥ virutaiḥ diśaḥ mātṛkām aṣṭa varga āḍhyām phalake bhuvi vā likhet śalya jñānam varga vaśāt pūrva ādi īśa antataḥ kramāt yavarge śavakīta ādi śavarge loham ādiśet prīkṣya ātmabhiḥ kara āpūraiḥ aṣṭa aṅgula mṛd antaraiḥ pāda ūnam khātam āpūrya sa jalaiḥ mudgara āhataiḥ liptām sama plavām tatra kārayitvā bhuvam guruḥ sāmānya arghya karaḥ yāyāt maṇḍapam toraṇa dvāḥpatīn iṣṭvā pratyak dvāreṇa saṃviśet kuryāt tatra ātma śuddhi ādi kuṇḍa maṇḍapa saṃskṛtim kalasam vardhanī saktam lokapāla śiva arcanam yajamāna anvitaḥ yāyāt śilānām snāna maṇḍapam śilāḥ prāsāda liṅgasya pāda dharma ādi sañjñakāḥ aṣṭa aṅgula ucchritāḥ śastāḥ catur asrāḥ kara āyatāḥ pāṣāṇānām śilāḥ kāryāḥ iṣṭakānām tad ardhataḥ prāsāde aśmaśilāḥ śaile iṣṭakāḥ iṣṭakā maye aṅkitāḥ nava vaktra ādyaiḥ paṅkajāḥ paṅkaja aṅkitāḥ āsām padmaḥ mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkhaḥ atha makaraḥ tathā samudraḥ ca iti pañcāmī nidhi kumbhāḥ krama adhas nandā bhadrā jayā pūrṇā ajitā ca aparājitā vijayā maṅgala ākhyā ca dharaṇī navamī śilā navānām tu yathāsaṅkhyam nidhi kumbhaḥ pūrṇaḥ tathā uttaraḥ āsanam prathamam dattvā tāḍya ullikhya śara aṇunā sarvāsām aviśeṣeṇa tanutreṇa avaguṇṭhanam mṛdbhiḥ gomaya yogāḥ mūtra kaṣāyaiḥ gandha vāriṇā astreṇa phaṭ antena malasnānam samācaret vidhinā pañcagavyena snānam pañcāmṛtena ca gandha toya antaram kuryāt nija nāma aṅkita aṇunā phala ratna suvarṇānām gośṛṅga salilaiḥ tatas svarṇa uttham āsanam da tvā nītvā yāgam pradakṣiṇam śayyāyām kuśa talpe vā hṛdayena niveśayet tattvāni nija mantreṇa tattva īśān ca hṛdā arcayet sthāneṣu puṣpa mālā ādi cihniteṣu yathākramam om hūm śivatattvāya namaḥ om hūm śivatattva adhipataye rudrāya namaḥ om hāṃ vidyā tattvāya namaḥ om hāṃ vidyā tattva adhipāya viṣṇave namaḥ om hāṃ ātma tattvāya namaḥ om hāṃ ātma tattva adhipataye brahmaṇe namaḥ kṣamā agni yajamāna arkān jala vāta indu khāni ca prati tattvam nyaset aṣṭau mūrtīḥ prati śilām śilām mahādevam ca bhīmam ca mūrtīśān ca yathākramāt om dharā mūrtaye namaḥ om dharā adhipataye namaḥ ityādi mantrān lokapālān yathāsaṅkhyam nija aṇubhiḥ indra ādīnām tu vījāni vakṣyamāṇa krameṇa tu lūm rūm śūm pūm vūm yūm mūm hūm kṣūm iti uktaḥ nava śilā pakṣaḥ śilā pañca padā tathā prati tattvam nyaset mūrtīḥ sṛṣṭyā pañca dharā ādikāḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ tathā rudraḥ īśvaraḥ ca sadāśivaḥ ete ca pañca mūrtīśāḥ yaṣṭavyāḥ tāsu pūrvavat om pṛthvī mūrtaye namaḥ om pṛthvī mūrti adhipataye brahmaṇe namaḥ iti ādi mantrāḥ sampūjya kalaśān pañca krameṇa nija nāmabhiḥ kuṇḍeṣu dhārikām śaktim vinyasya abhyarcya tarpayet tattva tattva adhipān mūrtīḥ mūrti īśān ca ghṛta ādibhiḥ tatas brahma aṃśa śuddhi artham mūla aṅgam brahmabhiḥ kramāt kṛtvā śata ādi pūrṇa antam prokṣyāḥ śānti jalaiḥ śilāḥ pūjayet ca kuśaiḥ spṛṣṭvā prati tattvam anukramāt sāṃnidhyam atha sandhānam kṛtvā śuddham punar nyaset om āṃ īṃ ātma tattva vidyā tattvābhyām namaḥ iti saṃspṛśet darbha mūla ādyaiḥ brahma aṅga ādi trayam kramāt om hāṃ um vidyā tattva śiva tattvābhyām namaḥ ghṛtena madhunā pūrṇān tāmra kumbhān sa ratnakān śilānām atha sarvāsām saṃsmaret adhidaivatāḥ vidyā rūpāḥ kṛta snānāḥ śilā ambarāḥ nyūna ādi doṣa moṣa artham vāstu bhūmeḥ ca śuddhaye yajet astreṇa mūrdha antam āhutīnām śatam śatam vāstu pūjā ādi vidhānam īśvaraḥ uvāca tatas prāsādam āsūtrya vartayet vāstu maṇḍapam kuryāt koṣṭha catuḥṣaṣṭim kṣetre veda asrake same koṇeṣu vinyaset vaṃśau rajjavaḥ aṣṭau vikoṇa gāḥ dvipadāḥ ṣaṣ padāḥ tāḥ tu vāstum tatra arcayet yathā ākuñcita kacam vāstum uttānam asura ākṛtim smaret pūjāsu kuḍya ādi niveśe uttarānanam jānunī kūrparau śakthi diśi vāta hutāśayoḥ paitryām pāda puṭe raudryām śiraḥ asya hṛdaye añjaliḥ asya dehe samārūḍhāḥ devatāḥ pūjitāḥ śubhāḥ aṣṭau koṇa adhipāḥ tatra koṇa ardheṣu aṣṭasu sthitāḥ ṣaṭpadāḥ tu marīci ādyāḥ dikṣu pūrva ādiṣu kramāt madhye catuṣpadaḥ brahmā śeṣāḥ tu padikāḥ smṛtāḥ samasta nāḍī saṃyoge mahāmarma anujam phalam trikuṭum maṇibandham ca su viśuddham padam tathā iti dvādaśa marmāṇi vāstoḥ bhitti ādiṣu tyajet sa ājyam akṣatam īśāya parjanyāya ambuja udakam dadīta atha jayantāya patākām kuṅkuma ujjvalām satyāya ghṛta godhūmam ājya bhaktam bhṛśāya ca vimāṃsam antarīkṣāya śuktum tebhyaḥ tu pūrvatas madhu kṣīra ājya sampūrṇām pradadyāt vahnaye śrucam lājān pūrṇam suvarṇa ambu vitathāya nivedayet dadyāt gṛha kṣate kṣaudram yamarāje pala odanam gandham gandharva nāthāya jihvām bhṛṅgāya pakṣiṇaḥ mṛgāya padma parṇāni yāmyām iti aṣṭa devatāḥ pitre tila udakam kṣīram vṛkṣa jam danta dhāvanam sugrīvāya diśet pūpān puṣpadantāya darbhakam ghṛtam guḍa odanam śeṣe rogāya ghṛtamaṇḍakān lājān vā paścima āśāyām devāṣṭakam iti īritam mārutāya dhvajam pītam nāgāya nāgakeśaram mukhye bhakṣyāṇi bhallāṭe mudga sūpam susaṃskṛtam somāya pāyasam sa ājyam śālūkamūṣaye diśet modakān brahmaṇaḥ prācyām ṣaṭpādāya marīcaye savitre rakta puṣpāṇi vahni adhas koṇa koṣṭhake tad adhas koṣṭhake dadyāt sāvitryai ca kuśa udakam dakṣiṇe candanam raktam ṣaṭpadāya vivasvate haridrā odanam indrāya rakṣaḥ dhaḥ krīṇa koṣṭhake varuṇyām ṣaṭpada āsīne mitre saṅuḍamodanam rudrāya ghṛta siddha annam vāyu koṇa adhare pade dadīta māṣa naivedyam ṣaṭpada sthe dharādhare śiva koṇa adhas tad vatsāya ca tad sthale kramāt dadyāt dadhi kṣīram pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ catuṣpade niviṣṭāya brahmaṇe madhma deśataḥ pañcagavya akṣata upetan carum sa ājyam nivedayet īśa ādi vāyu paryanta koṇeṣu atha yathākramam vāstu vāhye carakyā ādyāḥ catasraḥ pūjayet yathā carakyai sa ghṛtam māṃsam vidāryai dadhi paṅkaje tatas māṣa odanam prācyām skandāya vinivedayet aryamṇe dakṣiṇa āśāyām pūpān kṛsarayā yutān jambhakāya ca vāruṇyām āmiṣam rudhira anvitam udīcyām pilipiñjāya rakta annam kusumāni ca yajet vā sakalam vāstum kuśa dadhi akṣateḥ jalaiḥ tri padāḥ rajjavaḥ kāryāḥ ṣaṣ padāḥ ca vikoṇake īśa ādyāḥ pādikāḥ tasmin nāgadyāḥ ca dvi koṣṭha gāḥ ṣaṣ pada sthāḥ marīci ādyāḥ brahmā nava padaḥ smṛtaḥ nagara grāma kheṭa ādau vāstuḥ śatapadaḥ api vā vaṃśa dvayam koṇa gatam durjayam durdharam sadā grahāḥ skanda ādayaḥ tatra vijñeyāḥ ca eva ṣaṣ padāḥ carakya ādyāḥ bhūta padāḥ rajju vaṃśa ādi pūrvavat catuḥṣaṣṭi padaḥ brahmā marīci ādyāḥ ca devatāḥ catuḥpañcāśat padikā āpādi aṣṭau rasa agnibhiḥ īśāna ādyāḥ nava padāḥ skanda ādyāḥ śaktikāḥ smṛtāḥ jñeyaḥ vaṃśa sahasraiḥ tu vāstu maṇḍala gaḥ padaiḥ pañcaciṃśat padaḥ vāstuḥ vaitāla ākhyaḥ citau smṛtaḥ anyaḥ nava padaḥ vāstuḥ ṣoḍaśa aṅghriḥ tathā aparaḥ khāte vāstoḥ samam pṛṣṭhe nyāse brahmaśilā ātmake śāṣākasya niveśe ca mūrti saṃsthāpane tathā pāyasena tu naivedyam sarveṣām vā pradāpayet ukta anukte tu vai vāstuḥ pañca hasta pramāṇataḥ gṛha prāsāda mānena vāstuḥ śreṣṭhaḥ tu sarvadā śilā vinyāsa vidhānam īśvaraḥ uvāca īśa ādiṣu carakya ādyāḥ pūrvavat pūjayet vahis da tvā bhūta balim lagne śilā nyāsam anukramāt nakāra ārūḍha mūlena kumbhe asmin dhārayet śilām kumbhān aṣṭau sa bhadra ādīn dikṣu pūrva ādiṣu kramāt lokapāla aṇubhiḥ nyasya śvabhreṣu nyasta śaktiṣu śilāḥ teṣu atha nanda ādyāḥ krameṇa viniyojayet śambaraiḥ mūrti nāthānām yathā syuḥ bhitti madhyatas tāsu dharma ādikān aṣṭau koṇāt koṇam vibhāgaśaḥ subhadrā ādiṣu nanda ādyāḥ catasraḥ agni ādi koṇa gāḥ ajita ādyāḥ ca pūrva ādi jaya ādiṣu atha vinyaset brahmāṇam ca upari masya vyāpakam ca maheśvaram śilā pañcaka pakṣe api manāk uddiśyate yathā madhye pūrṇaśilā nyāsaḥ subhadra kalaśe ardhataḥ padma ādiṣu ca nanda ādyāḥ koṇeṣu agni ādiṣu kramāt om pūrṇe tvam mahā viśve sarva sandoha lakṣaṇe sarva sampūrṇam eva atra kuruṣva aṅgirasaḥ sute om nande tvam nandinī puṃsām tvām atra sthāpayāmi aham prāsāde tiṣṭha santṛptā yāvat candra arka tārakam āyuḥ kāmam śriyannande dehi vāsiṣṭha dehinām asmin rakṣā sadā kāryā prāsāde yatnataḥ tvayā om bhadre tvam sarvadā bhadram lokānām kuru kāśyapi āyuḥ dā kāma dā devi śrī pradā ca sadā bhava om jaye atra sarva dā devi śrī dā āyuḥ dā ca sadā bhava om jaye atra sarvadā devi tiṣṭha tvam sthāpitā maya sarvadā sarva deśa sthe tiṣṭha asmin viśva rūpiṇi pratiṣṭhā sāmagrī vidhānam īśvaraḥ uvāca vakṣye liṅga pratiṣṭhām ca prāsāde bhukti mukti dām vinā caitreṇa māgha ādau pratiṣṭhā māsa pañcake śuklapakṣe viśeṣeṇa kṛṣṇe vā pañcamandinam caturthīm navamīm ṣaṣṭhīm varjayitvā caturdaśīm śobhanāḥ tithayaḥ śa ṣāḥ krūra vāra vivarjitāḥ śatabhiṣā dhaniṣṭhā ārdrā anurodha uttara trayam rohiṇī śravaṇaḥ ca iti sthira ārambhe mahā udayāḥ lagnam ca kumbha siṃha ali tulā strī vṛṣa dhanvinām śastaḥ jīvaḥ nava ṛkṣeṣu sapta sthāneṣu sarvadā budhaḥ ṣaṣ aṣṭa diś sapta turyeṣu vinartum śitaḥ sapta ṛtu tridaśa ādi sthaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ bala daḥ sadā raviḥ daśa tri ṣaṣ saṃsthaḥ rāhuḥ tri daśa ṣaṣ gataḥ ṣaṣ tri sthāna gatāḥ śastāḥ manda aṅgāra arka ketavaḥ śubhrāḥ krūraḥ ca pāpāḥ ca sarve ekādaśa sthitāḥ eṣām dṛṣṭiḥ munau pūrṇā tu ārdhikī graha bhūtayoḥ pādikī rāma diś sthāne catur aṣṭau pāda varjitā pāda anyūna catur nāḍī bhogaḥ syāt mīna meṣayoḥ vṛṣa kumbhau ca bhuñjāte catasraḥ pāda varjitāḥ makaraḥ mithunam pañca cāpāli hari karkaṭāḥ pādīnāḥ ṣaḍ tulākanye ghaṭikāḥ sārdhapañca ca keśarī vṛṣabhaḥ kumbhaḥ sthirāḥ syuḥ siddhi dāyakāḥ carāḥ dhanuḥ tulā meṣāḥ dviḥsvabhāvāḥ tṛtīyakāḥ śubhaḥ śubha grahaiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śastaḥ lagnaḥ śubha āśritaḥ rājyam śauryam balam putrān yaśaḥ dharma ādikam bahu tri ekādaśa caturtha sthāḥ lagnāt pāpa grahāḥ śubhāḥ dhāmnaḥ pañcaguṇām bhūmim tyaktvā vā dhāna sammitām hastāt dvādaśa sopānāt kuryāt maṇḍam agratas eka āsyam catur āsyam vā raudryām dvi hasta uttarayā vṛddhyā śeṣam syāt maṇḍapa aṣṭakam vedī pāda antaram tyaktvā kuṇḍāni nava pañca vā ekam vā śiva kāṣṭhāyām prācyām vā tad guroḥ param muṣṭi mātram śata ardhe syāt śate lakṣe catuṣkāram kuṇḍam koṭi home aṣṭa hastakam ṣaṣ asram vāyave padmam saumye ca aṣṭa asrakam śive tiryakpāta śivam khātam ūrdhvam mekhalayā saha aṅgulaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ekā vā kuṇḍa ākārāḥ tu mekhalāḥ tāsām upari yoniḥ syāt madhye aśvattha dala ākṛtiḥ ucchrāyeṇa aṅgulam tasmāt vistāreṇa aṅgula aṣṭakam dairghyam kuṇḍa ardha mānena kuṇḍa kaṇṭha samaḥ adharaḥ pūrva agni yāmya kuṇḍānām yoniḥ syāt uttara ānanā pūrva ānanā tu śeṣāṇām aiśānye anyatarā tayoḥ kuṇḍānām yaḥ caturviṃśaḥ bhāgaḥ saḥ aṅgulaḥ iti atas plakṣa udumvaraka aśvattha vaṭa jāḥ toraṇāḥ kramāt śānti bhūti bala ārogya pūrva ādyāḥ nāmataḥ kramāt indrāyudha upamā raktā kṛṣṇā dhūmrā śaśi prabhā śukla ābhā hema varṇā ca patākā sphāṭika upamā pañca hastāḥ tad ardhāḥ ca dhvajāḥ dīrghāḥ ca vistarāḥ hasta pradeśitāḥ daṇḍāḥ dhvajānām pañca hastakāḥ valmīkāt danti danta agrāt tathā vṛṣabha śṛṅgataḥ padma ṣaṇḍāt varāhāt ca goṣṭhāt api catuṣpathāt mṛttikāḥ dvādaśa grāhyāḥ vaikuṇṭha iṣṭau pinākini kaṣāyapañcakam grāhyam ārtavam ca phala aṣṭakam tīrtha ambhāṃsi sugandhīni tathā sarva oṣadhī jalam śastam puṣpa phalam vakṣye ratna gośṛṅga vāri ca snānāya apāharet pañca pañcagavya amṛtam tathā sahasra śuṣiram kumbham maṇḍalāya ca rocanā śatam oṣadhi mūlānām vijayā lakṣmaṇā balā guḍūcī atibalā pāṭhā sahadevā śatāvarī ṛddhiḥ suvarcasā vṛddhiḥ snāne proktā pṛthak pṛthak yava godhūma vilvānām cūrṇāni ca vicakṣaṇaḥ vilepanam sa karpūram snāna artham kumbha gaṇḍakān khaṭvāñca tūlikā yugmam sa upadhānam sa vastrakam ghṛta kṣaudra yutam pātram kuryāt svarṇa śalākikām vardhanīm śiva kumbhañca lokapāla ghaṭān api ekam nidrā kṛte kumbham śānti artham kuṇḍa saṅkhyayā dvārapāla ādi dharma ādi praśānta ādi ghaṭān api vastu lakṣmī gaṇeśānām kalaśān aparān api dhānya puñja kṛta ādhārān sa vastrān sraj vibhūṣitān kumbha saṇḍakān iti cha kumbha khaṇḍakān iti ja sa hiraṇyān samālabdhān gandha pānīya pūritān pūrṇa pātra phala ādhārān pallava ādyān sa lakṣaṇān vikira artham tathā lājān jñāna khaḍgam ca pūrvavat sa apidhānām carusthālīm darvīm ca tāmra nirmitām ghṛta kṣaudra anvitam pātram pāda abhyaṅga kṛte tathā viṣṭarān triśatāt arbha dalaiḥ bāhu pramāṇakān tila pātram haviḥ pātram ardha pātram pavitrakam phala viṃśa aṣṭa mānāni ghaṭaḥ dhūpa pradānakam śruc śruvau piṭakam pīṭham vyajanam śuṣkam indhanam puṣpam patram gugglan ca ghṛtaiḥ daupān ca dhūpakam akṣatāni tri sūtrīn ca gavyam ājyam yavān tilān kuśāḥ śāntyai tri madhuram samidhaḥ daśa parvikāḥ bāhu mātra śruvam hastam arka ādi graha śāntaye samidhaḥ arka palāśa utthāḥ khādira āmārga pippalāḥ udumvara śamī dūrvā kuśa utthāḥ śatam aṣṭa ca tad abhāve yava tilāḥ gṛha upakaraṇam tathā sthālī darvī pidhāna ādi deva ādibhyaḥ aṃśuka dvayam mudrā mukuṭa vāsāṃsi hāra kuṇḍala kaṅkaṇān kuryāt ācārya pūjā artham vitta śāṭhyam vivarjayet tad pāda pāda hīnā ca mūrtibhṛt astra jāpinām pūjā syāt jāpibhiḥ tulyā vipra daivajña śilpinām vajra arka śāntau nīla atinīla muktāphalāni ca puṣpa padma ādi rāgam ca vaidūryam ratnam aṣṭamam śrīkhaṇḍam sāri kaṅkuṣṭham śaṅkṣinī hi oṣadhī guṇaḥ hema tāmra mayam raktam rājatam ca sa kāṃsyakam śīsakam ca iti lohāni haritālam manaḥśilā gairikam hemamākṣīkam pāradaḥ vahnigairikam godhūmān sa tilān māṣān mudgān api āharet yavān nīvārān śyāmakān evam brīhayaḥ api aṣṭa kīrtitāḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca snātvā nitya dvayam kṛtvā praṇava argha karaḥ guruḥ kṣānti ādi toraṇān tatra pūrvavat pūjayet kramāt pradakṣiṇa kramāt eṣām śākhāyām dvārapālakān prāci nandi mahākālau yāmye bhṛṅgi vināyakau vāruṇe vṛṣabha skandau devī caṇḍau tatas uttare tad śākhā mūla deśa sthau praśānta śiśirau ghaṭau parjanya aśoka nāmānau bhūtam sañjīvana amṛtau bhānu trayam yugam vedaḥ lakṣmīḥ gaṇapatiḥ tathā iti devā makhāgāre tiṣṭhanti pratitoraṇam vighna saṅgha apanodāya kratoḥ saṃrakṣaṇāya ca vajram śaktim tathā daṇḍam khaḍgam pāśam dhvajam gadām om phaṭ namaḥ om phaṭ dvāḥstha śaktaye phaṭ namaḥ iti ādi mantraiḥ kumudaḥ kumudākṣaḥ ca puṇḍarīkā utha vāmanaḥ śaṅku karṇaḥ sarva netraḥ su mukhaḥ su pratiṣṭhitaḥ dhvaja aṣṭadevatāḥ pūjyāḥ pūrva ādau bhūta koṭibhiḥ kālam karālinam ṣaṣṭham eka aṅghrim bhīmam aṣṭakam kambala āstṛteṣu varṇeṣu vaṃśa sthūṇāsu anukramāt sadāśiva pada vyāpi maṇḍapam dhāma śāṅkaram patākā śakti saṃyuktam tattva dṛṣṭyā avalokayet divya antarikṣa bhūmiṣṭha vighnān utsārya pūrvavat praviśet paścima dvārā śeṣa dvārāṇi darśayet pradakṣiṇa kramāt gatvā niviṣṭaḥ vedi dakṣiṇe uttara abhimukhaḥ kuryāt bhūtaśuddhim yathā purā antaryāgam viśeṣa arghyam mantra dravya ādi śodhanam kurvīta ātmanaḥ pūjām pañcagavya ādi pūrvavat om haṃ hāṃ mūrtīḥ tad īśvarān tatra pūrvavat viniveśayet tad vyāpakam śivam sa aṅgam śiva hastam ca mūrdhani ātmānam mūrtipaiḥ sārdham sraj vastra kusuma ādibhiḥ bhūṣayitvā śivaḥ asmi iti dhyātvā boghāsim uddharet catuṣpada anta saṃskāraiḥ saṃskuryāt makha maṇḍapam āsanīkṛtya vardhanyām vāstu ādīn pūrvavat yajet sva dikṣu kalaśa ārūḍhān lokapālān anukramāt vāha āyudha ādi saṃyuktān pūjayet vidhinā yathā airāvata gaja ārūḍham svarṇa varṇam kirīṭinam sahasranayanam śakram vajrapāṇim vibhāvayet sapta arciṣam ca vibhrāṇam akṣamālām kamaṇḍalum jvālā mālā ākulam raktam śakti hastam aja āsanam mahiṣa stham daṇḍa hastam yamam kāla analam smaret rakta netram svara ārūḍham khaḍga hastam ca nairṛtam varuṇam makare śvetam nāgapāśa dharam smaret vāyum ca hariṇe nīlam kuveram megha saṃsthitam triśūlinam vṛṣe ca īśam cakriṇam brāhmāṇam haṃsa gam dhyāyet caturvaktram caturbhujam śiva ājñām śrāvayet kumbham bhrāmayet ātma pṛṣṭha gam śivam sthira āsanam kumbhe śastra artham ca dhruva āsanam pūjayitvā yathāpūrvam spṛśet udbhava mudrayā ebhiḥ saṃśrāvya rakṣā artham kumbhe khaḍgam niveśayet dīkṣā sthāpanayoḥ kumbhe sthaṇḍile maṇḍale athavā kuṇḍanābhim puraskṛtya niniṣṭhāḥ mūrti dhāriṇaḥ guroḥ ādeśataḥ kuryuḥ nija kuṇḍeṣu saṃskṛtim paṭheyuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ śāntim sva śākhā vedapāragāḥ śrīsūktam pāvamānīḥ ca maitrakam ca vṛṣākapim devavratantu bhāruṇḍam jyeṣṭhasāma rathantaram puruṣam gītim etāni sāmavedī tu dakṣiṇe rudram puruṣasūktam ca śloka adhyāyam viśeṣataḥ brāhmaṇam ca yajurvedī paścimāyām samuccaret nīlarudram tathā atharvī ca ācāryaḥ ca agnim utpādya pratikuṇḍam pradāpayet vahneḥ pūrva ādikān bhāgān pūrva kuṇḍa āditaḥ kramāt dhūpa dīpa carūṇām ca dadīta agnim samuddharet homam kṛtvā tu mantra jñaḥ pūrṇām dattvā śubha āvahām pūrvavat carukam kṛtvā prati kuṇḍam nivedayet yajamāna alaṅkṛtāḥ tu vrajeyuḥ snāna maṇḍapam bhadrapīṭhe nidhāya īśam tāḍayitvā avaguṇṭhayet snāpayet pūjayitvā tu mṛdā kāṣāya vāriṇā go mūtraiḥ gomayena api vāriṇā ca antarā antarā bhasmanā gandha toyena phaṭ anta astreṇa vāriṇā deśikaḥ mūrtipaiḥ sārdham kṛtvā kāraṇa śodhanam dharma japtena sañchāṭya pīta varṇena vāsasā tatra datta āsanāyām ca śayyāyām sanniveśya ca śalākayā suvarṇasya akṣiṇī śastrakarmaṇā añjayet lakṣma kṛt paścāt śāstra dṛṣṭena karmaṇā kṛta karmā ca śastreṇa lakṣmī śilpī samutkṣipet tri aṃśāt ardhā utha pāda ardhāt ardhāyāḥ sarva kāma prasiddhi artham śubham lakṣma avatāraṇam liṅga dīrgha vikāra aṃśe tri bhaktam bhāga varṇanāt yavasya nava bhaktasya bhāgaiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ āvṛtā evam aṣṭa aṃśa vṛddhyā tu liṅge sa ardha kara ādike bhavet aṣṭa yavā pṛthvī gambhīrā atra ca hāstike evam aṣṭa aṃśa vṛddhyā tu liṅge sa ardha kara ādike bhavet aṣṭa yavā pṛthvī gambhīrāt nava hāstike śāmbhaveṣu ca liṅgeṣu pāda vṛddheṣu sarvatas rekhā api tri aṃśa vṛddhitaḥ sarveṣu ca bhavet sūkṣmām liṅga mastaka mastakam lakṣma kṣetra iṣṭadhā bhakte mūrdhni bhāga dvaye śubhe rekhā trayeṇa sambaddham kārayet pṛṣṭadeśa gam svarūpam lakṣaṇam teṣām prabhā ratneṣu nirmalā lakṣmaṇa uddhāra rekhām ca ghṛtena madhunā tathā arcayet ca tatas liṅgam snāpayitvā mṛd ādibhiḥ śilpinan toṣayitvā tu dadyāt gām gurave tatas liṅgam dhūpa ādibhiḥ prācyam gāyeyuḥ bhartṛ gāḥ trayaḥ savyena ca apasavyena sūtreṇa atha kuśena vā smṛtvā ca rocanam da tvā kuryāt nirmañjana ādikam guḍa lavaṇa dhānyāka dānena visṛjet ca tāḥ guru mūrti dharaiḥ sārdham hṛdā vā praṇavena vā snāpayet pañcagavyena pañcāmṛta puraḥsaram virūkṣaṇam kaṣāyaiḥ ca sarva oṣadhi jalena vā śubhra puṣpa phala svarṇa ratna śṛṅga yava udakaiḥ tīrtha udakena gāṅgena candanena ca vāriṇā kṣīrārṇava ādibhiḥ kumbhaiḥ śiva kumbha jalena ca virūkṣaṇam vilepan ca su gandhaiḥ candana ādibhiḥ rakta rūpeṇa rakṣā tilaka pūrvakam dravyaiḥ stuti ādibhiḥ tuṣṭam arcayet puruṣāṇunā samācamya hṛdā devam brūyāt utthīyatām prabho maṇḍape paścima dvāre śayyāyām viniveśayet paścime piṇḍikā antasya nyaset brahma śala anta dā utthāpya ukta āsane liṅgam śirasā pūrva mastakam dadyāt dhūpam ca sampūjya tathā vāsāṃsi varmaṇā gṛha upakṛti naivedyam hṛdā dadyāt sva śaktitaḥ ghṛta kṣaudra yutam pātram abhyaṅgāya pada antike deśikaḥ ca sthitaḥ tatra ṣaṭtriṃśat tattva sañcayam māyā apadeśa śakti antan turya āśā aṣṭa aṃśa vartulam tatra ātma tattva vidyā ākhyam śivam tu ekaśas pratibhāgeṣu brahma viṣṇu hara adhipān vinyasya mūrti mūrti īśān pūrva ādi kramataḥ yathā kṣmā vahniḥ yajamāna arka jala vāyu niśākarān ākāśa mūrti rūpān tān nyaset tad adhināyakān mahādevañca bhīmañca mantrāḥ tad vācakāḥ ime lava śaṣa caya sāḥ ca hakāraḥ ca tri mātrikaḥ praṇavaḥ hṛdaya arṇuḥ vā mūlamantraḥ athavā kvacid pañca kuṇḍa ātmake yāge mūrtīḥ pañca athavā nyaset pṛthivī jala tejāṃsi vāyum ākāśam eva ca kramāt tad adhipān pañca brahmāṇam dharaṇodharam rudram īśam sadā ākhyan ca sṛṣṭi nyāyena mantra vid mumukṣoḥ vā nivṛtta ādyāḥ ajāta ādyāḥ tad īśvarāḥ śuddhe ca ātmani vidyeśāḥ aśuddhe loka nāyakāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ mūrtipāḥ ca eva bhoginī mantranāyakāḥ pañcaviṃśat tathā eva aṣṭa pañca trīṇi yathākramam tad īśānām indra ādīnām tatas yathā om hāṃ śakti tattvāya namaḥ iti ādi om hāṃ śakti tattva adhipāya namaḥ iti ādi om hāṃ kṣmā mūrtaye namaḥ om hāṃ kṣmā mūrti adhīśāya śivāya namaḥ iti ādi om hāṃ pṛthivī mūrtaye namaḥ om hāṃ mūrti adhipāya brahmaṇe namaḥ iti ādi om hāṃ śivatattva adhipāya rudrāya namaḥ iti ādi nābhi kandāt samuccārya ghaṇṭā nāda visarpaṇam brahma ādi kāraṇa tyāgāt dvādaśānta samāśritam dvādaśāntāt samānīya niṣkalam vyāpakam śivam aṣṭatriṃśat kalā upetam sahasra kiraṇa ujjvalam sarva śakti mayam sa aṅgam dhyātvā liṅge niveśayet jīva nyāsaḥ bhavet evam liṅge sarva artha sādhakaḥ piṇḍikā ādiṣu tu nyāsaḥ procyate sāmpratam yathā piṇḍikām ca kṛta snānām viliptām candana ādibhiḥ pañcaratna ādi saṃyuktām liṅgasya uttaratas sthitām kṛta snāna ādikān tatra liṅga mūle śilām nyaset kṛta snāna ādi saṃskāram śakti antam vṛṣabham tathā praṇava pūrvam hum pūm hrīṃ madhyāt anyatamena ca kriyāśakti yutām piṇḍīm śilām ādhara rūpiṇīm rakṣāyai lokapālān ca sa āyudhān yājayet vahis om hūm hraṃ kriyā śaktaye namaḥ om hūm hrāṃ haḥ mahāgaurī rudra dayite svāhā iti ca piṇḍikāyām om hāṃ ādhāra śaktaye namaḥ om hāṃ vṛṣabhāya namaḥ dhārikām dīptimatī ugrā jyotsnā ca etāḥ bala utkaṭāḥ tathā dhātrī vidhātrī ca nyaset vā pañcanāyikāḥ vāmā jyeṣṭhā kriyā jñānā bedhā tisrī ithavā nyaset kriyā jñānā tathā icchā ca pūrvavat śānti mūrtiṣu tamaḥ mohā kṣamī niṣṭhā mṛtyuḥ māyā bhava jvarāḥ kriyājñānā tathā bādhā adhināyikā ātma ādi triṣu tattveṣu tīvra mūrtiṣu vinyaset atra api piṇḍikā brahmaśilā ādiṣu yathāvidhi evam vidhāya vinyāsam gatvā kuṇḍa antikam tatas kuṇḍa madhye maheśānam mekhalāsu maheśvaram kriyāśaktim tathā anyāsu nādam oṣṭhe ca vinyaset ghaṭam sthaṇḍila vahni īśaiḥ viśantī sūrya mārgeṇa niḥsarantīm samudgatām punar ca śūnya mārgeṇa viśatīm svasya cintayet sampūjya dhārikām śaktim kuṇḍe santarpya ca kramāt tattva tattva īśvarāḥ murtīḥ mūrtīḥ śān ca ghṛta ādibhiḥ śatam sahasram ardham vā pūrṇayā saha homayet tattva tattva īśvarā mūrtiḥ mūrti īśān ca kareṇukān santarpya śaktim kumbha ambhaḥ prokṣite kuśa mūlataḥ liṅga mūlam ca saṃspṛśya japeyuḥ homa saṅkhyayā sannidhānam hṛdā kuryuḥ varmaṇā ca avaguṇṭhanam evam saṃśodhya brahma ādi viṣṇu anta ādi viśuddhaye kuśa madhya agra yogena liṅga madhya agrakam spṛśet om hāṃ haṃ om om om eṃ om bhūṃ bhūṃ vāhya mūrtaye namaḥ o hāṃ vām āṃ om āṃ ṣāṃ om bhūṃ bhūṃ vā vahni mūrtaye namaḥ pañca mūrti ātmake pi evam sandhānam hṛdaya ādibhiḥ śilā piṇḍaḥ vṛṣeṣu evam pūrṇā chinnam su saṃvaraiḥ bhāga abhāga viśuddhi artham homam kuryāt śata ādikam nyūna ādi doṣa moṣāya śivena aṣṭa adhikam śatam vidhi pūrṇam apūrṇam vā sva śaktyā āpūrya gṛhyatām om hrīṃ śāṅkari pūraya svāhā iti piṇḍikāyām atha liṅge nyaset jñānī kriyā ākhyam pīṭha vigrahe ādhāra rūpiṇīm śaktim nyaset brahmaśilā upari nibadhya sapta rātram vā pañca rātram tri rātrakam vinā adhivāsanam yāgaḥ kṛtaḥ api phala pradaḥ sva mantraiḥ pratyaham deyam āhutīnām śatam śatam śiva pratiṣṭhā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca prātar nitpa vidhim kṛtvā dvārapāla prapūjanam aṣṭa muṣṭikayā liṅgam vahnim san parpya ca kramāt śiva ajñātaḥ tatas gacchet prāsādam śastram uccaran tad gatān prakṣipet vighnān hum phaṭ anta śara aṇunā na madhye sthāpayet liṅgam bedha doṣa viśaṅkayā kiñcid īśānam āśritya śilām madhye niveśayet mūlena tām ananta ākhyām sarva ādhāra svarūpiṇīm sarvagām sṛṣṭi yogena vinyaset acalām śilām athavā anena mantreṇa śivasya āsana rūpiṇīm hraṃ laṃ hrīṃ svāhā tvayā śiva ājñayā śakte sthātavyam iha santatam vajra ādīni ca ratnāni tathā uśīra ādika oṣadhīḥ lohān hema ādi kāṃsi antān haritāla ādikān tathā dhānya prabhṛti śastrān ca pūrva muktān anukramāt pūrva ādiṣu ca garteṣu nyaset ekaikaśas kramāt hema jam tāra jam kūrmam vṛṣam vā dvāra sammukham sarit taṭa mṛdā yuktam parvata agra mṛdā athavā pṛthivīm rājatīm yat vā yat vā hema samudbhavām sarva vīja suvarṇābhyām samāyuktām vinikṣipet suvarṇam kṛśarā yuktam padma nālam tatas nyaset śvabhram ācchādya vastreṇa tanutreṇa astra rakṣitam śevena vā śilā śvabhra saṅga doṣa nivṛttaye śastreṇa vā śatam samyak juhuyāt pūrṇayā saha samutthāpya hṛdāt evam āsanam maṅgala ādibhiḥ caturbhiḥ saha kartavyā devayajñasya pṛṣṭhatas liṅgam saṃsthāpya da tvā arghyam prāsādam sanniveśayet dvāra bandhe śikhā śūnye tad ardhena atha tad ṛte varjayan dvāra saṃsparśam dvāreṇa eva maheśvaram atha pīṭhe ca saṃsthāpya liṅgam dvārasya sammukham tūrya maṅgala nirgheṣaiḥ dūrvā akṣata samanvitam samuttiṣṭham hṛdā iti uktvā mahāpāśupatam paṭhet apanīya ghaṭam śvabhrāt deśikaḥ mūrtipaiḥ saha laya antam mūlam uccārya spṛṣṭvā śvabhre niveśayet ardhena vā aṣṭama aṃśena sarvasya atha praveśanam vidhāya sīsakam nābhi dīrghābhiḥ su samāhitaḥ śvabhram brūyāt sthirībhava iti ca tatas liṅge sthirībhūte dhyātvā sakala rūpiṇam mūlam uccārya śakti antam sṛṣṭyā ca niṣkalam nyaset sthāpyamānam yadā liṅgam yāmyām diśam atha āśrayet tad tad digīśa mantreṇa pūrṇa antam dakṣiṇa anvitam juhuyāt mūlamantreṇa bahurūpeṇa vā śatam kuñca anyeṣu api doṣeṣu śivaśāntim samāśrayet yuktam nyāsa ādibhiḥ liṅgam kurvan evam na doṣa bhāj pīṭhabandham atas kṛtvā lakṣaṇasya aṃśa lakṣaṇam gaurī mantram layam nītvā sṛṣṭyā piṇḍīn ca vinyaset sampūrya pārśva saṃsiddhim vālukā vajra lepanam tatas mūrti dharaiḥ sārdham guruḥ śāntim ghaṭa ūrdhvatas saṃsthāpya kalaśaiḥ anyaiḥ tadvat pañcāmṛta ādibhiḥ umā maheśa mantrābhyām tau spṛśet liṅga mudrayā tatas tri tattva vinyāsam ṣaṣ arcā ādi puraḥsaram kṛtvā mūrtim tad īśānām aṅgānām brahmaṇām atha jñānī liṅge kriyāpīṭhe vinā āsya snāpayet tatas candra arka tārakam yāvat mantreṇa śaiva mūrtipaiḥ praṇamya iva vahis gatvā hṛdā vā praṇavena vā saṃsthāpya vṛṣabham paścāt pūrvavat valim ācaret nyūna ādi doṣa moṣāya tatas mṛtyu jitā śatam śivena sa śivaḥ hutvā śānti artham pāyasena ca jñāna ajñāna kṛtam yat ca tat pūraya mahā vibho hiraṇya paśu bhūmi ādi gīta vādya ādi hetave dānam mahā utsavam paścāt kuryāt dina catuṣṭayam caturthe ihani pūrṇān ca carukam bahurūpiṇā dina catuṣṭayam yāvat tat nirmālī anta ūrdhataḥ nirmālya apanayam kṛtvā snāpayitvā tu pūjayet pūjā sāmānya liṅgeṣu kāryā sādhāraṇa aṇubhiḥ vihāya liṅga caitanyam kuryāt sthāṇu visarjanam asādhāraṇa liṅgeṣu kṣamasva iti visarjanam nityaḥ utha sarvagaḥ ca eva avināśī dṛṣṭaḥ eva ca ete guṇāḥ maheśasya sannidhānāya kīrtitāḥ om namaḥ śivāya sthiraḥ bhava iti āhutīnām kramaḥ saṃsnāpya tat dvitīyam tu kartṛ snānāya dhārayet da tvā balim samācamya vahis gacchet śiva ājñayā jagatī vāhyatas caṇḍam aiśānyān diśi mandire pūrvavat nyāsa homa ādi vidhāya dhyāna pūrvakam aṅgāni pūrva yuktāni brahmāṇī tu arcanā yathā evam sadyojātāya om hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ om viṃ vāmadevāya hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ om buṃ aghorāya hrūṃ phaṭ namaḥ om tatpuruṣāya vaumi īśānāya ca hrūṃ phaṭ nyūna adhikam ca yat kiñcid kṛtam ajñānataḥ mayā abhyarcya caṇḍam sa sutam yajamānam hi bhāryayā vitta śāṭhyam vinā dadyāt bhū hiraṇya ādi dakṣiṇām mūrtimān vidhivat paścāt jāpakān brāhmaṇān tathā devajñam śilpinam prārcya dīna anātha ādi bhojayet kṣamasva nātha tat sarvam kāruṇya ambunidham mama pratiṣṭhā puṇya sadbhāvam sphurat tāraka saprabham tatas pāśa pata upetam praṇamya parameśvaram guruḥ vastra ādi saṃyuktam gṛhṇīyāt yāga maṇḍapam sarva upakaraṇam śilpī tathā snāpana maṇḍapam ādi varṇasya bhedāt vā su tattva vyāpti bhāvitāḥ kṣetrapāḥ kinnara ādyāḥ ca pṛthivī tattvam āśritāḥ snānam sarasvatī lakṣmī nadīnām ambhasi kvacid aṇḍa vṛddhi pradhāna antam tri tattvam brahmaṇaḥ padam tanmātra ādi pradhāna antam padam etat trikam hareḥ nāṭya īśa gaṇa mātṝṇām yakṣa īśa śara janmanām aṇḍa jāḥ śuddhavidyā antam padam gaṇapateḥ tathā māyā aṃśa deśa śakti anatam śivā śiva upta rociṣām padam īśvara paryantam vyakta arcāsu ca kīrtitam kūrma ādyam kīrtitam yat ca yat ca ratna ādi pañcakam pratikṣipet pīṭha garte ca pañcabrahmaśilām vinā ṣaḍbhiḥ vibhājite garte tyaktvā bhāvam ca pṛṣṭhatas sthāpanam pañcama aṃśe ca yadi vā vasu bhājite dhāraṇābhiḥ viśuddhiḥ syāt sthāpane lepa citrayoḥ snāna ādi mānasam tatra śilā ratna ādi veśanam pūjā nirambubhiḥ puṣpaiḥ yathā citram na duṣyati bhaga trayeṇa bhāga aṃśaḥ bhavet bhāga dvayena vā sṛṣṭi mantreṇa saṃskāraḥ vidhivat sphāṭika ādiṣu kiñca brahmaśilā ratna prabhūteḥ ca a nivedanam yojanam piṇḍikāyāḥ ca manasā parikalpayet svayambhū vāṇa liṅga ādau saṃskṛtau niyamaḥ na hi snāpanam saṃhitā mantraiḥ nyāsam homan ca kārayet nadī samudra rohāṇām sthāpanam pūrvavat matam aihikam mṛṇmayam liṅgam piṣṭaka ādi ca takṣaṇāt kṛtvā sampūjayet śuddham sīkṣaṇa ādi vidhānataḥ samādāya tatas mantrān ātmānam sannidhāya ca viṣṇu ādi sthāpanam ca eva pṛyak mantraiḥ samācaret gaurī pratiṣṭhā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca vakṣye gaurī pratiṣṭhām ca pūjayā sahitām śṛṇu maṇḍapa ādyam puras yat ca saṃsthāpya ca adhiropayet śayyāyāḥ antān ca vinyasya mantrān mūrti ādikān guha ātma vidyā śiva antam ca kuryāt īśa niveśanam śaktim parām tatas nyasya hutvā japtvā ca pūrvavat sandhāya ca tathā piṇḍīm kriyāśakti svarūpiṇīm sa deśa vyāpikām dhyātvā nyasta ratna ādikām tathā evam saṃsthāpya tām paścāt devīn tasya anniyojayet para śakti svarūpa antām sva aṇunā śakti yogataḥ tatas nyaset kriyāśaktim pīṭhe jñānam ca vigrahe tatas upi vyāpinīm śaktim samāvāhya niyojayet ambikām śiva nāmnīm ca samālabhya prapūjayet om ādhāra śaktaye namaḥ om kūrmāya namaḥ om skandāya ca tathā namaḥ om hrīṃ nārāyaṇāya namaḥ om aiśvaryāya namaḥ om aṃ adhas chadanāya namaḥ om padmāsanāya namaḥ om ūrdhva chadanāya namaḥ om padmāsanāya namaḥ atha sampūjyāḥ keśavāḥ tathā om hrīṃ karṇikāya namaḥ om kṣaṃ puṣkarākṣebhyaḥ iha arcayet om hāṃ puṣṭyai hrīṃ ca jñānāyai hrūṃ kriyāyai tatas namaḥ om nālāya namaḥ ruṃ dharmāya namaḥ ruṃ jñānāya vai namaḥ om vairāgyāya vai namaḥ om vai adharmāya namaḥ om ruṃ ajñānāya vai namaḥ sūrya pratiṣṭhā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca vakṣye sūrya pratiṣṭhām ca pūrvavat maṇḍapa ādikam snāna ādikam ca pūrva ukta vidhinā tatas vidyām āsana śayyāyām sa aṅgam vinyasya bhāskaram śuddhi ādi pūrvavat kṛtvā piṇḍīm saṃśodhya pūrvavat sva aṇunā vidhivat sūryam śakti antam sthāpayet guruḥ svāmi antam athavā ādityam pāda antam nāma dhārayet sūrya mantrāḥ tu pūrva uktāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ sthāpane api ca dvāra pratiṣṭhā kathanam īśvaraḥ uvāca dvāra āśrita pratiṣṭhāyāḥ vakṣyāmi vidhim api atha dvāra aṅgāni kaṣāya ādyaiḥ saṃskṛtya śayane nyaset mūla madhya agra bhāgeṣu trayam ātma ādi sa īśvaram ratna ādi pañcakam nyasya śānti homam vidhāya ca yava siddhārthaka ākrāntāḥ ṛddhi vṛddhi mahātilāḥ rocanā ruc vacaḥ dūrvā prāsāda adhas ca poṭalīm dvāram uttaratas kiñcid āśritam san niveśayet śiva makāśa deśe ca vyāpakam sarvamaṅgale dvāra āśritān ca talpa ādīn kṛta yuktaiḥ sva nāmabhiḥ juhuyāt śatam ardham vā dviguṇam śaktitas thavā nyūna ādi doṣa moṣa artham hetitaḥ juhuyāt śatam prāsāda pratiṣṭhā uvāca śuka nāśā samāptau tu pūrva vedyāḥ ca madhyatas cūta ādi pallavānām ca kṛtī kṛtyam ca vinyaset pūrakeṇa samādāya sakalīkṛta vigrahaḥ sarva ātma bhinna ātmānam sva aṇunā svānta mārutaḥ dvādaśāntāt samādāya sphurat vahni kaṇā upamam vigrahan tad guṇānām ca bodhakam ca kalā ādikam kṣāntam vāgīśvaram tat tu brātam tatra niveśayet daśa nāḍīḥ daśa prāṇān indriyāṇi trayodaśa tad adhipān ca saṃyojya praṇava ādyaiḥ sva nāmabhiḥ vidyeśān prerakān śambhum vyāpinaḥ ca suvarṇa ādi udbhavam yat vā puruṣam puruṣa anugam pañcagavya kaṣāya ādyaiḥ pūrvavat saṃskṛtan tatas śayyāyām kumbham āropya dhyātvā rudram umāpatim sannidhānāya homañca praokṣaṇam sparśanam japam dhvaja āropaṇam īśvaraḥ uvāca pratiṣṭhā ca yathā uddiṣṭā tathā skanda vadāmi te taḍāga ardha praveśāt vā yat vā sava ardha veśanāt aiṣṭake dāru jaḥ śūlaḥ śaila je dhāmni śaila jaḥ vaiṣṇava ādau ca cakra āḍhyaḥ kumbhaḥ syāt mūrti mānataḥ īśaśūlaḥ samākhyātaḥ mūrdhni liṅga samanvitaḥ vījapūraka yuktaḥ vā śiva śāstreṣu tadvidhaḥ bhavet vā daṇḍamānaḥ tu yadi vā tat yadṛcchayā mahādhvajaḥ samākhyātaḥ yaḥ tu pīṭhasya veṣṭakaḥ uttama ādi krameṇa eva vijñeyaḥ śūribhiḥ tatas vaṃśa jaḥ śāla jātiḥ vā sa daṇḍaḥ sarva kāma daḥ ayam āropyamāṇaḥ tu bhaṅgam āyāti vai yadi rājñaḥ niṣṭam vijānīyāt yajamānasya vā tathā dvārapāla ādi pūjām ca mantrāṇām tarpyaṇan tathā vidhāya cūlakam daṇḍam snāpayet astra mantrataḥ mṛdu kaṣāya ādibhiḥ snānam prāsādam kārayet tatas vilipya rasam ācchādya śayyāyām nyasya pūrvavat cūḍake liṅga vaṇa nyāsaḥ na ca jñānam na ca kriyā viśeṣa arthā caturthī ca na kuṇḍasya kalpanā daṇḍe tayā artha tattvam ca vidyā tattvam dvitīyakam niṣkalam ca śivam tatra nyasya aṅgāni prapūjayet anyathā api kṛtam yat ca dhvaja saṃskāraṇam kvacid prāsāde kārite sthāne sraj vastra ādi vibhūṣite homa ādikam vidhāya atha śivam sampūjya pūrvavat kuṣmāṇḍa hāṭakau pīṭhe pātāla narakaiḥ saha brahmāṇdakam idam dhyātvā jaṅghā tān ca vibhāvayet sarvāvaraṇa sañjñam ca vṛddhayoni avṛka anvitam yoga aṣṭaka samāyuktam nāśāvidhi guṇatrayam paṭa stham puruṣam siṃham vāmaḥ ca paribhāvayet mañjarī vedikāyām ca vidyā ādika catuṣṭayam kaṇṭhe māyām sa rudrān ca vidyāḥ ca amalasārake jaṭājūṭam ca tam vidyāt śūlam candra ardha rūpakam śakti trayam ca tatra eva daṇḍe nādam vibhāvya ca dhvaje ca kuṇḍalīm śaktim iti dhāmni vibhāvayet jagatyā vā atha sandhāya liṅgam piṇḍikayā athavā dhāma pradakṣiṇīkṛtya labhate phalam īhitam adhipān śastra yuktān ca rakṣaṇāya nibodhayet nyūna ādi doṣa śānti artham hutvā da tvā ca digbalim gurave dakṣiṇām dadyāt yajamānaḥ divam vrajet pratimā liṅga vedīnām yāvantaḥ paramāṇavaḥ jīrṇa uddhāraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca jīrṇa ādīnām ca liṅgānām uddhāram vidhinā vade saṃpuṭam sphuṭitam vyaṅgam liṅgam iti evam ādikam ityādi duṣṭa liṅgānām yojyā piṇḍī tathā vṛṣaḥ cālitam calitam liṅgam atyartham viṣama sthitam diḍmūḍham pātitam liṅgam madhyastham patitam tathā tatas anyatra api saṃsthāpya vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā susthitam dusthitam vā api śiva liṅgam na cālayet śatena sthāpanam kuryāt sahasreṇa tu cālanam pūjā ādibhiḥ ca saṃyuktam jīrṇa ādyam api susthitam yāmye maṇḍapam īśe vā pratyak dvāra eka toraṇam vidhāya dvāra pūjā ādi sthaṇḍile mantra pūjanam brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu śambhum vijñāpayet tatas duṣṭa liṅgam idam śaṃbhoḥ śāntiḥ uddhāraṇasya ced adhitiṣṭhasva mām śiva evam vijñāpya deveśam śānti homam samācaret madhu ājya kṣīra dūrvābhiḥ mūlena aṣṭa adhikam śatam tatas liṅgam ca saṃsthāpya pūjayet sthiṇḍile tathā om vyāpaka īśvarāya iti nāṭyantam śiva vādinā om vyāpakam hṛdaya īśvarāya namaḥ om vyāpaka īśvarāya śirase namaḥ iti ādi aṅga mantrāḥ sattvaḥ kopī iha yaḥ kopi liṅgam āśritya tiṣṭhati liṅgan tyaktvā śiva ājñābhiḥ yatra iṣṭam tatra gacchatu sahasram pratibhāge ca tatas pāśupata aṇunā hutvā śāntyambunā prokṣya spṛṣṭvā kuśaiḥ japet tatas aṣṭamūrtīśvarān liṅga piṇḍikā saṃsthitān guruḥ visṛjya svarṇa pāśena vṛṣa skandha sthayā tathā rajvā vadhvā tayā nītvā śivam antam gṛṇan janaiḥ tṛptaye dikpatīnām ca vāstu śuddhau śatam śatam rakṣām vidhāya tad dhāmni mahā pāśupatā tatas jīrṇam vā api athavā bhagnam vidhinā api na cālayet eṣaḥ eva vidhiḥ kāryaḥ jīrṇa dhāma samuddhṛtau saṅkoce maraṇam proktam tu dhana kṣayaḥ tad dravyam śreṣṭha dravyam vā tat sa kāryam tad pramāṇakam prāsāda lakṣaṇam īśvaraḥ uvāca vakṣye prāsāda sāmānya lakṣaṇam te śikhadhvaja adri bhāgena garbhaḥ syāt piṇḍikā pāda vistarāt pañca bhāgīkṛte kṣetre intar bhāge tu piṇḍikā suṣiram bhāga vistīrṇam bhittayaḥ bhāga vistarāt garbhaḥ bhāgena vistīrṇaḥ bhāga dvayena piṇḍikā vistārāt dviguṇaḥ vā api sa pāda dviguṇaḥ api vā nemiḥ prāsādasya samantataḥ cāmuṇḍam bhairavam teṣu nāṭya īśam ca niveśayet prāsāda ardhena devānām aṣṭau vā caturaḥ api vā pradakṣiṇām vahis kuryāt prāsāda ādiṣu vā ādityāḥ pūrvatas sthāpyāḥ skanda ugniḥ vāyu gocare evam yama ādayaḥ nyasyāḥ svasyāḥ svasyām diśi sthitāḥ caturdhā śikharam kṛtvā śukanāsā dvi bhāgikā tṛtīye vedikā tu agneḥ sa kaṇṭhaḥ malasārakaḥ vairājaḥ puṣpakaḥ ca anyaḥ kailāsaḥ maṇikaḥ tathā triviṣṭha pañca pañca eva meru mūrdhani saṃsthitāḥ vṛttaḥ vṛtta āyataḥ ca anyaḥ hi aṣṭa asraḥ ca api pañcamaḥ śrīvatsaḥ ca iti vairājya anvavāye ca samutthitāḥ balabhī gṛha rājaḥ ca śālāgṛham ca mandiram prabhavaḥ śivikā veśma navā ete puṣpaka udbhavāḥ vardhanī vā anyaḥ uṣṇīṣaḥ śaṅkhaḥ ca kalasaḥ tathā sva vṛkṣaḥ ca tathā api ete vṛttāḥ kailāsa sambhavāḥ gajaḥ utha vṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaḥ garutmān nṛkṣa nāyakaḥ bhūṣaṇaḥ bhūdharaḥ ca an nye śrījayaḥ pṛthavīdharaḥ vṛtta āyatāt samudbhūtāḥ navā ete maṇika āhvayāt citram svastika khaḍgam ca gadā śrīkaṇṭhaḥ eva ca nagarāṇām imāḥ sañjñāḥ lāṭa ādīnām imāḥ tathā grīvā ardhena unnatam cūlam pṛthulam ca vibhāgataḥ daśadhā vedikāṅkṛtvā pañcabhiḥ skandha vistaraḥ tribhiḥ kaṇṭham tu kartavyam caturbhiḥ tu pracaṇḍakam dikṣu dvārāṇi kāryāṇi na vidikṣu kadācana piṇḍikā koṇa vistīrṇā madhyama antā hi udāhṛtā ucchrāyāḥ dviguṇāḥ teṣām anyathā vā nigadyate ṣaṣṭyā adhikāt samārabhya aṅgulānām śatāt iha uttamāni api catvāri dvārāṇi daśa hānitaḥ ucchrāyāt pāda vistīrṇāḥ viśākhāḥ tat uduṃvare dvi pañca sapta navabhiḥ śākhābhiḥ dvāram iṣṭa dam adhas śākhā caturtha aṃśe pratīhārau niveśayet mithunaiḥ pāda varṇābhiḥ śākhā śeṣam vibhūṣayet prāsāda gṛha śilā ādi mārga viddheṣu bandhanam sabhā biddhe na dāridryam varṇa biddhe nirākṛtiḥ ulūkhalena dāridryam śilā biddhena śatru tā chedāt utpāṭanāt vā api tathā prākāra lakṣaṇāt sīmāyāḥ dviguṇa tyāgāt bedha doṣaḥ na jāyate īśvaraḥ uvāca nagara grāma durga ādyāḥ gṛha prāsāda vṛddhaye prāc āsyāḥ daśadhā nāḍyāḥ tāsām nāmāni ca bruve śāntā yaśovatī kāntā viśālā prāṇa vāhinī uttarā dvādaśa anyāḥ ca ekāśīti aṅghri kārikā hariṇī suprabhā lakṣmīḥ vibhūtiḥ vimalā priyā jayā jvālā viśokā ca smṛtāḥ tatra pādataḥ īśa ādi aṣṭa aṣṭakam dikṣu yajet īśam dhanañjayam śakram arkam tathā satyam bhṛśam vyoma ca pūrvatas kṛtāntam atha gandharvam bhṛgam mṛgan ca dakṣiṇe pitaram dvārapālam ca sugrīvam puṣpadantakam varuṇam daityaśeṣau ca yakṣmāṇam paścime sadā nava antaḥ pada gaḥ brahmā pūjya ūrdhe ca ṣaṣ aṅghi gāḥ brahma īśa antara koṣṭha stha māyā ākhyāntu pad dvaye tad adhas cāpa vat sa ākhyam kendra antareṣu ṣaṭpade sāvitrī tad adhas dvi aṃśe vivasvān ṣaṭpade tu adhas tad adhas dvi aṅghri gam yakṣma ṣaṣ saumyeṣu dharādharam carakīm skanda vikaṭam vidārīm pūtanām kramāt jammam pāpam pilipiccham yajet īśa ādi vāhyataḥ ekāśīpadam veśma maṇḍapaḥ ca śata aṅghrikaḥ pūrvavat devatāḥ pūjyāḥ brahmā tu ṣoḍaśa aṃśake marīciḥ ca vivasvān ca mitram pṛthvīdharaḥ tathā daśa koṣṭha sthitāḥ dikṣu tu anye beśa ādi koṇa gāḥ daitya mātā tathā īśa agnī mṛga ākhyau pitarau tathā pāpayakṣma anilau devāḥ sarve sārdha aṃśake sthitāḥ yat pādya ukaḥ pravakṣyāmi saṅkṣepeṇa kramāt guha sa diś viṃśat karaiḥ dairghyāt aṣṭāviṃśati vistarāt śiśira āśrayaḥ śiva ākhyaḥ ca rudra hīnaḥ sadā ubhayoḥ rudra dvi guṇitāḥ nāhāḥ pṛthu ṣṇobhiḥ vinā tribhiḥ sāvitraḥ sa ālayaḥ kuḍyāḥ anyeṣām pṛthak kuḍya sūtra samā pṛthvī vīthī bhedāt anekadhā bhadre tulyam ca vīthībhiḥ dvāra vīthī vinā agratas śrī jayam pṛṣṭhatas hīnam bhadroyam pārś cayoḥ vinā sāmānya anātha gṛham vakṣye sarveṣām sarva kāma dam eka dvi tri catur śālam aṣṭa śālam yathākramāt śiva āsyam ambupa asya eṣa indra āsye yama sūryakam prāc saumya sthe ca daṇda ākhyam prāc yāmye vāta sañjñakam āpya indau gṛhavalī ākhyam triśūlam tad vinardhi kṛt syāt su kṣetram vṛddhi dāyakam yāmye hīne bhavet śūlī tri śālam vṛddhi kṛt param indra ādi kramataḥ vacmi dhvaja ādi aṣṭau gṛhāṇi aham prakṣāla anusraga āvāsam agnau tasya mahānasam yāmye rasakriyā śayyā dhanuḥ śastrāṇi rakṣasi saumye dhana paśū kuryāt īśe dīkṣā vara ālayam svāmi hasta mitam veśma vistāra āyāma piṇḍikam triguṇam hasta saṃyuktam kṛtvā aṣṭa aṃśaiḥ hṛtam tathā sarva nāśa karam veśma madhye ca ante ca saṃsthitam tad madhe maṇḍapaḥ śastaḥ samaḥ vā dviguṇa āyataḥ pratyak āpye ca indu yame haṭṭe eva gṛha āvalī ekaika bhavana ākhyāni dikṣu aṣṭa aṣṭaka saṅkhyayā īśa ādi aditi kāntāni phalāni eṣām yathākramam bhayam nārī calatvam ca jayaḥ vṛddhiḥ pratāpakaḥ dharmaḥ kaliḥ ca prāc dvāreṣu aṣṭasu dhruvam dāhaḥ asukham suhṛd nāśaḥ dhana nāśaḥ mṛtiḥ dhanam śilpi tvam tanayaḥ syāt ca yāmya dvāra phala aṣṭakam āyuḥ prāvrājya śasyāni dhana śānti artha saṅkṣayāḥ śoṣam bhogam ca apatyam ca jala dvāra phalāni ca rogaḥ mad ārti mukhya tvam ca artha āyuḥ kṛśa tā matiḥ mānaḥ ca dvārataḥ pūrve kramāt nagara ādi vāstuḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca nagara ādika vāstuḥ ca vakṣye rājya ādi vṛddhaye yojanam yojana ardham vā tad artham sthānam āśrayet īśa ādi triṃśat padake pūrva dvāram ca sūryake gandharvābhyām dakṣiṇe syāt vāruṇye paścime tathā saumya dvāram saumya pade kāryāḥ haṭṭāḥ tu vistarāḥ yena ibha ādi sukham gacchet kuryāt dvāram tu ṣaṣ karam vajrasūcīmukham na iṣṭam sakṛt dvi tri samāgamam cāpa ābham vajra nāga ābham pura ārambhe hi śānti kṛt prārcya viṣṇu hara arka ādīn natvā dadyāt balim balī dakṣiṇe nṛtya vṛttīnām veśyā strīṇām gṛhāṇi ca naṭānām cakrikā ādīnām kaivarta ādeḥ ca nairṛte rathānām āyudhānām ca kṛpāṇām ca vāruṇe śauṇḍikāḥ karma adhikṛtāḥ vāyavye parikarmaṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ yatayaḥ siddhāḥ puṇyavantaḥ ca ca uttare phala ādi ādi vikrayiṇaḥ īśāne ca vaṇij janāḥ pūrvatas ca bala adhyakṣāḥ āgneye vividham balam strīṇām ādeśinaḥ dakṣe kāṇḍārān nairṛte nyaset paścime ca mahā amātyān koṣa pālān ca kārukān uttare daṇḍanāthān ca nāyaka dvija saṅkulān pūrvatas kṣatriyān dakṣe vaiśyān śūndrān ca paścime dikṣu vaidyān vājinaḥ ca balāni ca caturdiśam pūrveṇa caraliṅgī ādīn śmaśāna ādīni dakṣiṇe paścime go dhana ādyañca kṛṣi kartṝn tathā uttare nyaset mlecchān ca koṇeṣu grāma ādiṣu tathā smṛtim śriyam vaiśravaṇam dvāri pūrve tau paśyatām śriyam deva ādīnām paścimatas pūrva āsyāni gṛhāṇi hi pūrvatas paścima āsyāni dakṣiṇe ca uttara ānanān nākeśa viṣṇu ādi dhāmāni rakṣā artham nagarasya ca pūrvāyām śrī gṛham proktam āgneyyām vai mahānasam śanayam dakṣiṇasyāntu nairṛtyām āyudha āśrayam bhojanam paścimāyāntu vāyavyām dhānya saṅgrahaḥ uttare dravya saṃsthānam aiśānyām devatāgṛham catur śālam tri śālam vā dvi śālam ca eka śālakam catur śāla gṛhāṇām tu śālā alindaka bhedataḥ śata dvayam tu jāyante pañcāśat pañca teṣu api tri śālāni tu catvāri dvi śālāni tu pañcadhā ekaśālāni catvāri ekālindāni vacmi ca aṣṭāviṃśat alindāni gṛhāṇi nagarāṇi ca ṣaḍ alindāni viṃśā eva aṣṭābhiḥ viṃśaḥ eva hi aṣṭa alindam bhavet evam nagara ādau gṛhāṇi hi vakṣye bhuvanakoṣam ca pṛthvīdvīpa ādi lakṣaṇam agnidhraḥ ca agnibāhuḥ ca vapuṣmān dyutimān tathā jyotiṣmān daśamaḥ teṣām satyanāmā sutaḥ abhavat priyabrata sutāḥ khyātāḥ sapta dvīpān dadau pitā vapuṣmate śālmalañca jyotiṣmate kuśāhvayam krauñcadvīpam dyutimate śākam bhavyāya dattavān puṣkaram savanāya adāt agnīdhre adāt sute śatam jambūdvīpam pitā lakṣam nābheḥ dattam himāhvayam hemakūṭam kimpuruṣe harivarṣāya naiṣadham ilāvṛte meru madhye ramye nīla acala śritam bhadrāśvāya ca bhadrāśvam ketumālāya paścimam śālagrāme tapaḥ taptvā yayau viṣṇoḥ layam nṛpaḥ yāni kumpuruṣa ādyāni hi aṣṭa varṣāṇi sattama teṣām svābhāvikī siddhiḥ sukha prāyā hi ayatnataḥ jarā mṛtyu bhayam na asti dharma adharmau yuga ādikam na adhamam himāt deśāt tu na abhitas ṛṣabhaḥ merudevyāt ca ṛṣabhāt bharataḥ abhavat ṛṣabhaḥ datta śrīḥ putre śālagrāme bharataḥ datta lakṣmīkaḥ śālagrāme harim gataḥ parameṣṭhī tatas tasmāt pratīhāraḥ tad anvayaḥ tasya putraḥ mahā vīryaḥ dhīmān tasmāt ajāyata tvaṣṭā tvaṣṭuḥ ca virajā rajaḥ tasya api abhūt sutaḥ kṛta tretā ādi sargeṇa sargaḥ svāyambhuvaḥ smṛtaḥ bhuvana koṣaḥ jambū plakṣa āhvayau dvīpau śālmaliḥ ca aparaḥ mahān kuśaḥ krauñcaḥ tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraḥ ca iti saptamaḥ ete dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ tu sapta saptabhiḥ āvṛtāḥ caturaśīti sāhasraḥ bhūyiṣṭhaḥ ṣoḍaśāt virāj dvātriṃśat mūrdhni vistarāt ṣoḍaśa adhas sahasravān bhūyas tasya asya śailaḥ asau karṇikā ākāra saṃsthitaḥ himavān hemakūṭaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca asya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṅgo ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ lakṣa pramāṇau dvau madhye daśa hīnāḥ tathā apare bhāratam prathamam varṣan tatas kimpuruṣam smṛtam uttarāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva yathā vai bhāratam tathā ilāvṛtam mahābhāga catvāraḥ ca atra parvatāḥ viṣkambhāḥ racitāḥ meroḥ yojana ayuta vistṛtāḥ pūrveṇa mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaḥ ca uttare smṛtaḥ ekādaśa śata āyāmāḥ pādapāḥ giri ketavaḥ jambūdvīpa iti sañjñā syāt phalam jambā gaja upamam jambūnadī rasena asya astu idam jāmbūnadam param supārśvaḥ pūrvatas meroḥ ketumālaḥ tu paścime vanam caitraratham pūrve dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ aruṇodam mahābhadram saṃśitodam sa mānasam śita ābhaḥ cakramuñja ādyāḥ pūrvatas keśara acalāḥ dakṣiṇa indreḥ trikūṭa ādyāḥ śiśi vāsa mukhāḥ jale śaṅkhakūṭa ādayaḥ saumye merau ca brahmaṇaḥ purī caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānām ca dikṣu ca indra ādi lokapālānām samantāt brahmaṇaḥ puras viṣṇu pādāt plāvayitvā candram svargāt patanti api pūrveṇa śītāḥ bhadrāśvāt śailāt śailāt gata arṇavam prayāti sāgaram kṛtvā sapta bhedā atha paścimam ā nīla niṣadha āyāmau mālyavat gandhamādanau bhāratāḥ ketumālāḥ ca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravaḥ tathā patrāṇi loka padmasya maryādā śaila vāhyataḥ jaṭharaḥ devakūṭaḥ ca maryādāparvatau ubhau tau dakṣiṇa uttara āyāmau ā nīla niṣadha āyatau aśīti yojana āyāmau arṇava antar vyavasthitau niṣadhaḥ pāripātraḥ ca maryādāparvatau ubhau pūrva pañca āyatau etau arṇava antar vyavasthitau jāṭhara ādyāḥ ca maryādāśailāḥ meroḥ caturdiśam keśara ādiṣu yāḥ droṇyaḥ tāsu santi purāṇi hi lakṣmī viṣṇu agni sūrya ādi devānām muni sattama bhaumānām svarga dharmāṇām na pāpāḥ tatra yānti ca bhārate kūrma rūpī ca matsya rūpaḥ kuruṣu api kimpuruṣa ādi aṣṭasu kṣudh bhīti śoka ādikam na ca catturviṃśati sāhasram prajāḥ jīvanti anāmayāḥ kṛta ādi kalpanā nā asti bhaumāni ambhāṃsi nā ambudāḥ sarveṣu eteṣu varṣeṣu sapta sapta kula acalāḥ nadyaḥ ca śataśas tebhyaḥ tīrtha bhūtāḥ prajajñire bhārate yāni nīrthāni tāni tīrthāni vacmi te tīrthamāhātmyam māhātmyam sarva tīrthānām vakṣye yat bhakti mukti dam pratigrāhāt upāvṛttaḥ laghu āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ a datvā kāñcanam gāḥ ca daridraḥ nāma jāyate puṣkaram paramam tīrtham sānnidhyam hi trisandhyakam daśa koṭi sahasrāṇi tīrthānām vipra puṣkare devāḥ prāptāḥ siddhim atra snātāḥ pitṛ sura arcakāḥ puṣkare duṣkaram gantum puṣkare duṣkaram tapaḥ duṣkaram puṣkare dānam vastum ca eva su duṣkaram tatra vāsāt japat śrāddhāt kulānām śatam uddharet jambumārgam ca tatra eva tīrthantaṇḍulikāśramam karṇāśramam koṭitīrtham narmadā cārvudam param tīrtham carmaṇvatī sindhuḥ somanāthaḥ prabhāsakam piṇḍārakam dvārakā ca gomatī sarva siddhi dā bhūmitīrtham brahmatuṅgam tīrtham pañcanadam param bhīmatīrtham giri indram ca devikā pāpa nāśinī tīrtham vinaśanam puṇyam nāgodbhedam agha ardanam tīrtham kumārakoṭiḥ ca sarvadānīritāni ca kurukṣetram gamiṣyāmi kurukṣetre vasāmi aham yaḥ evam satatam brūyāt saḥ amalaḥ prāpnuyāt divam tatra viṣṇu ādayaḥ devāḥ tatra vāsāt harim vrajet pāṃśavaḥ api kurukṣetre nayanti paramām gatim dharmatīrtham suvarṇa ākhyam gaṅgādvāram anuttamam tīrtham kaṇakhalam puṇyam bhadrakarṇa hradam tathā gaṅgā sasvatī saṅgam brahmāvartam agha ardanam bhṛgutuṅgam ca kubjāmram gaṅgodbhedam aghāntakam kapālamocanam tīrthantīrtharājam prayāgakam gomatī gaṅgayoḥ saṅgam gaṅgā sarvatra nāka dā tīrtham rājagṛham puṇyam śālagrāmam aghāntakam vaṭeśam vāman tīrtham kālikāsaṅgam uttamam lauhityam karatoya ākhyam śoṇam ca atha ṛṣabham param godāvarī tuṅgabhadrā kāveraḥ varadā nadī tāpī payoṣṇī revā ca daṇḍaka araṇyam uttamam kālañjaram muñjavaṭan tīrtham sūrpārakam param mandākinī citrakūṭam śṛṅgavera puram param avantī paramam tīrtham ayodhyā pāpa nāśanī gaṅāmāhātmyam gaṅāmāhātmyam ākhyāsye sevyā sā bhukti mukti dā yeṣām madhye yāti gaṅgā te deśāḥ pāvanāḥ varāḥ gatiḥ gaṅgā tu bhūtānām gatim anveṣatām sadā gaṅgā tārayate ca ubhau vaṃśau nityam hi sevitā cāndrāyaṇa sahasrāt ca gaṅgā ambhaḥ pānam uttamam gaṅām saṃsevya sarva yajña phalam labhet yāvat asthi ca gaṅgāyām tāvat svarge sa tiṣṭhati gaṅgā tīrtha samudbhūta mṛd hārī saḥ darśanāt sparśanāt pānāt tathā gaṅgā iti kīrtanāt punāti puṇyapuruṣān śataśītha sahasraśas prayāgamāhātmyam prayāge brahma viṣṇu ādyāḥ deva muni varāḥ sthitāḥ saritaḥ sāgarāḥ siddhāḥ gandharva sara apsaḥ tathā tatra trīṇi agnikuṇḍāni teṣām madhye tu jāhnavī gaṅgā yamunayoḥ madhyam pṛthivyāḥ jaghanam smṛtam prayāgam sa pratiṣṭhānam kambala aśvatarau ubhau tīrtham bhogavatī ca eva vedī proktā prajāpateḥ tatra vedāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca mūrtimantaḥ prayāgake prayāge dānam śrāddham japya ādi ca akṣayam daśa tīrtha sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi koṭyaḥ tathā aparāḥ teṣām sānnidhyam atra eva prayāgam param antatas gavām koṭi pradānāt yat tri aham snānasya tat phalam prayāge māgha māse tu evam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ sarvatra sulabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu durlabhā gaṅādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgara saṅgame urvaśī pulinam ramyam tīrtham sandhyāvataḥ tathā koṭītīrtham ca aśvamedham gaṅgā yamunam uttamam mānasam rajasā hīnam tīrtham vāsarakam param vārāṇasīmāhātmyam vārāṇasī param tīrtham gauryai prāha maheśvaraḥ bhukti mukti pradam puṇyam vasatām gṛṇatām harim gaurīkṣetram na muktam vai avimuktam tatas smṛtam aśmanā caraṇau hatvā vaset kāśīn na hi tyajet hariḥ candram param guhyam guhyam āmnātaka īśvaram japyeśvaram param guhyam guhyam śrīparvatam tathā mahālayam param guhyam bhṛguḥ caṇḍeśvaram tathā varaṇā ca nadī ca āsīt tayoḥ madhye vārāṇasī atra snānam japaḥ homaḥ maraṇam deva pūjanam śrāddham dānam nivāsaḥ ca yat yat syāt bhukti mukti dam narmadā ādika māhātmyam vakṣye iham narmadām parām sadyas punāti gāṅgeyam darśanāt vāri nārmadam ṣaṣṭiḥ tīrtha sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi koṭyaḥ tathā aparāḥ kāverīsaṅgamam puṇyam śrīparvatam atas śṛṇu gaurī śrī rūpiṇī tepe tapaḥ tām abravīt hariḥ samantāt yojana śatam mahā puṇyam bhaviṣyati atra dānam tapaḥ japyam śrāddham sarvam atha akṣayam maraṇam śiva lokāya sarva dam tīrtham uttamam gayāmāhātmyam gayāmāhātmyam ākhyāsye gayā tīrtha uttama uttamam uktaḥ kṣīrābdhi gaḥ viṣṇuḥ pālaya asmān gaya asurāt tathā iti uktvā gataḥ viṣṇuḥ daityam dṛṣṭvā na vā harim gatāḥ śūnyā mahī svarge devāḥ brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ gatāḥ ūcuḥ harim devāḥ śūnyā bhūḥ tridivam hare yāga artham daitya deham tvam prārthaya tridaśaiḥ saha atithiḥ prārthayāmi tvā andeham yāgāya pāvanam yāgam cakāra calite dehi pūrṇāhutim vibhuḥ punar brahmā abravīt viṣṇum pūrṇa kāle asuraḥ acalat śiṣṇuḥ dharmam atha āhūya prāha deva mayīm śilām gadādharaḥ madīyā atha mūrtiḥ sthāsyati sa amaraiḥ dharmaḥ śilām deva mayīm tat śrutvā adhārayat parām yā dharmāt dharmavatyām ca jātā dharma vratā sutā marīciḥ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ tām uvāha tapaḥ nvitām yathā hariḥ śriyā reme gauryā śambhuḥ tathā tayā kuśa puṣpa ādi araṇyāt ca ānīya ati śrama anvitaḥ bhuktvā dharma vratām prāha pāda saṃvāhanam kuru pāda saṃvāhanam kurve brahmā pūjyaḥ guroḥ guruḥ vicintya pūjayāmāsa brahmāṇam ca arhaṇa ādibhiḥ marīciḥ tām apaśyat sa śaśāpa ukti vyatikramāt pāda abhyaṅgam parityajya tvad guruḥ pūjitaḥ mayā adoṣā aham yatas tvam hi śāpam prāpsyasi śaṅkarāt dharmavratā pṛthak śāpam dhārayitvā agrim adhyagāt tapaḥ cacāra varṣāṇām sahasrāṇi ayutāni ca tatas viṣṇu ādayaḥ devāḥ varam brūhi iti ca abruvan devāḥ ūcuḥ dattaḥ marīcinā śāpaḥ bhaviṣyati na ca anyathā śilā pavitrā deva aṅghri lakṣitā tvam bhaviṣyasi sarva deva mayī puṇyā niḥ hi brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca rudra ādyāḥ gaurī lakṣmī mukhāḥ surāḥ
